
-----title
大名 (出生地)
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=951&endYear=958')">951-958年</a>　开始读书。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e35a427f085b4162b7a1ef140c6d0dc5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e35a427f085b4162b7a1ef140c6d0dc5");'><span id='e35a427f085b4162b7a1ef140c6d0dc5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=960&endYear=960')">960年</a>　是年父任元成令。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>　始学章句。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=962&endYear=962')">962年</a>　始习韩愈文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=963&endYear=963')">963年</a>　习韩文，父上丞相书求官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ef9f71c273f14988969d302f326dac31_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ef9f71c273f14988969d302f326dac31");'><span id='ef9f71c273f14988969d302f326dac31_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=965&endYear=972')">965-972年</a>，19-26岁</div><div id='ef9f71c273f14988969d302f326dac31' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=965&endYear=965')">965年五月十日</a>　父卒，遂奉灵柩归京返魏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=965&endYear=965')">965年</a>　始作古文，颇为好事者讥议，而志向弥坚。作品：《应责》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《应责》系柳开早年号召古文的纲领，然以文道合一，特重道统，持论偏颇。）</span><div id='poem_1147943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应责</a><span class='authorDate'>（965年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147943")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147943'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147943'>或责曰：「子处今之世，好古文与古人之道，其不思乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147943_comment'></div>苟思之，则子胡能食乎粟，衣乎帛，安于众哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147943_comment'></div>众人所鄙贱之，子独<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1147943", 1147943, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>贵尚</span>之，孰从子之化也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147943_comment'></div>忽焉将见子穷饿而死矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147943_comment'></div>柳子应之曰：「于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147943_comment'></div>天生德于人，圣贤异代而同出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147943_comment'></div>其出之也，岂以汲汲于富贵，私丰于己之身也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147943_comment'></div>将以区区于仁义，公行千古之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147943_comment'></div>己身之不足，道之足，何患乎不足？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147943_comment'></div>道之不足，身之足，则孰与足？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147943_comment'></div>今之世与古之世同矣，今之人与古之人亦同矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147943_comment'></div>古之教民，以道德仁义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147943_comment'></div>今之教民，亦以道德仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147943_comment'></div>是今与古胡有异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147943_comment'></div>古之教民者，得其位，则以言化之，是得其言也，众从之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147943_comment'></div>不得其位，则以书于后，传授其人，俾知圣人之道易行，尊君，敬长，孝乎父，慈乎子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147943_comment'></div>大哉斯道也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147943_comment'></div>非吾一人之私者也，天下之至公者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147943_comment'></div>是吾行之，岂有过哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147943_comment'></div>且吾今恓恓草野，位不及身，将以言化于人，胡从于吾矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147943_comment'></div>故吾著书自广，亦将以传授于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147943_comment'></div>子责我以好古文，子之言何谓为古文？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147943_comment'></div>古文者，非在辞涩言苦，使人难读诵之，在于古其理，高其意，随言短长，应变作制，同古人之行事，是谓古文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147943_comment'></div>子不能味吾书，取吾意，今而视之，今而诵之，不以古道观吾心，不以古道观吾志，吾文无过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147943_comment'></div>吾若从世之文也，安可垂教于民哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147943_comment'></div>亦自愧于心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147943_comment'></div>欲行古人之道，反类今人之文，譬乎游于海者乘之以骥，可乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147943_comment'></div>苟不可，则吾从于古文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147943_comment'></div>吾以此道化于民，若鸣金石于宫中，众岂曰丝竹之音也，则以金石而听之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147943_comment'></div>食乎粟，衣乎帛，何不能安于众哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147943_comment'></div>苟不从于吾，非吾不幸也，是众人之不幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147943_comment'></div>吾岂以众人之不幸，易我之幸乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147943_comment'></div>纵吾穷饿而死，死即死矣，吾之道岂能穷饿而死之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147943_comment'></div>吾之道，孔子、孟轲、扬雄、韩愈之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147943_comment'></div>吾之文，孔子、孟轲、扬雄、韩愈之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147943_comment'></div>子不思其言，而妄责于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147943_comment'></div>责于我也即可矣，责于吾之文、吾之道也，即子为我罪人乎」！</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1147943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=966&endYear=967')">966-967年</a>　事迹不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年</a>　自号“东郊野夫”，著《东郊书》，后又焚之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年</a>　建来显亭，为文记之。作品：《来贤亭记》<div id='poem_1147951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>来贤亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147951")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147951'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147951'>人之学善文章，行事烈烈，代为之称者，虽前古而生，孰不欲愿与之知，企慕恨乎己之后时而出不及也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147951_comment'></div>观夫同世而偕立，并能而齐名，则反有不相识相知者，亦有识而不知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147951_comment'></div>吾观乎斯二者，经史子集之中，或绝言而不相谈，或曾言而不相周，有之多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147951_comment'></div>吾未尝静坐思之不为惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147951_comment'></div>是夫当时力不相及者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147951_comment'></div>是夫当时义不相宾者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147951_comment'></div>因而诲之，吾所以异是于世矣，乃构此亭在东郊，厥有意乎，命曰「来贤」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147951_comment'></div>吾欲举天下之人与吾同道者，悉相识而相知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147951_comment'></div>有能闻于吾者，吾欲信而来于是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147951_comment'></div>有未闻于吾者，吾欲知而来于是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147951_comment'></div>有先达于吾者，吾欲趋而来于是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147951_comment'></div>有后进于吾者，吾欲诱而来于是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147951_comment'></div>有务胜于吾者，吾欲让而来于是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147951_comment'></div>有推退于吾者，吾欲尊而来于是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147951_comment'></div>大者吾将仰之，小者吾将俯之，贵者吾将奉之，贱者吾将崇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147951_comment'></div>极吾心而尽于世，合吾道而比于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147951_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147951_comment'></div>若曰子将来贤之徒于人，人将来贤之名于子者，吾又非斯志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147951_comment'></div>盖欲夫是亭也，不独如前言而已耳，亦将化今而警古矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1147951_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年</a>　有文。作品：《东郊野史传》九十篇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《答梁拾遗改名书》载其凡九十三篇，总三十卷。）</span><div id='poem_1147964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东郊野夫传</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147964")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147964'>东郊野夫，肩愈者，名也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147964_comment'></div>绍先者，字也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147964_comment'></div>不云其族氏者，姓在中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147964_comment'></div>家于魏，居邻其郭之门左，故曰东郊也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147964_comment'></div>从而自号之，故曰野夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子邑处而曰郊，士流而曰野，无乃失乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147964_comment'></div>野夫对曰：「吾以为郊，子以为邑矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147964_comment'></div>吾以为野，子以为士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147964_comment'></div>吾宁知郊不为邑，士不为野，是果能质其名之在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147964_comment'></div>苟不果，吾斯不失矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147964_comment'></div>野夫居于家则称曰东郊，出于旅则称曰魏郊，以别内外之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147964_comment'></div>野夫性浑然，朴而不滞，淳而不昧，柔知其进，刚识其退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147964_comment'></div>推之以前不难其行，揖之于后不忿其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147964_comment'></div>来者虽仇而不拒，去者虽亲而不追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147964_comment'></div>大抵取人之长，弃人之短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147964_comment'></div>利不能诱，祸不能惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147964_comment'></div>晦乎若无心，茫乎若无身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147964_comment'></div>不以天地之大独为大，不以日月之明独为明，风雷不疾其变，岳渎不险其固，人莫之识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147964_comment'></div>与其交者，无可否，无疑忌，贤愚贵贱，视其有分，久与之往还，益见深厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147964_comment'></div>或持其无赖之心者，谓其真若鄙愚人也，即事以欺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147964_comment'></div>复有以一得，便再以其二三而谋从计其利，虽后己或自败，野夫与始亦无暂异，竟不言之，然终未有能出其度内者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147964_comment'></div>父兄有以诲而勉之，野夫哑尔笑而对曰：「小儿辈徒劳耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147964_comment'></div>吾尝捕虎于穴，挟其门以利刃，彼于内虽奋跃万变，奈吾当尔隘之阨乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147964_comment'></div>矧若类之蠢蠢哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147964_comment'></div>或有宾自远方至，即倾产以待之，遽与之宴笑寝处无少间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147964_comment'></div>父兄有曰：「汝胡尔为也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147964_comment'></div>一何太疏易乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147964_comment'></div>殊不察其彼之人为若是，无乃不可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147964_comment'></div>野夫曰：「彼人耳，吾人耳，又何间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147964_comment'></div>且天地之中孰有内外也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147964_comment'></div>四海之人皆我之亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147964_comment'></div>己茍有所分别，虽父母兄弟，果肯不以他心待之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147964_comment'></div>己茍无所间于人，即孰忍间于吾乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147964_comment'></div>父兄以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147964_comment'></div>宾既告返，即解衣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>质钱</span>以赆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147964_comment'></div>或贫饿于时，有若可哀者，虽食，减口以遗，恐恐然犹虑不得与之久济矣，不虞其己之反困也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子居贫贱而务施仁义，司马氏之所讥也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147964_comment'></div>野夫对曰：「吁哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147964_comment'></div>君子计人之急，岂谋己乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147964_comment'></div>当贫贱而能施诸仁义，斯所难也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147964_comment'></div>当贵富而将施之，即孰不为能乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147964_comment'></div>且司马氏盖异其君子者耳，所以著书而多离于夫子之旨焉，或退处士而进奸雄，或先黄老而后六经，盖例若此也，吾所耻耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147964_comment'></div>或有结仇相忿者，野夫曰：「汝来前！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147964_comment'></div>何故深憾乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147964_comment'></div>且汝谋彼以复怨，彼作报以图尔，两祸不泯，循环然将何止也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147964_comment'></div>汝无恨他人之不我善，盖自不能善于人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147964_comment'></div>汝茍周于人，即何有不汝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>丰美</span>乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147964_comment'></div>汝见盗之为行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147964_comment'></div>其为残贼污恶，虽父母亦不能容耳，反有同类而相感者，尚皆殒身拒害，有以甘心为交之终始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147964_comment'></div>盖无他，能感彼心以尽我诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147964_comment'></div>盗之犹若是，矧汝辈皆良民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147964_comment'></div>慎勿若此也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147964_comment'></div>仇闻之者，或相解去焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147964_comment'></div>野夫家苦贫，无继夕之粮，无顺时之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147964_comment'></div>年始十五六，学为章句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147964_comment'></div>越明年，赵先生指以韩文，野夫遂乐得而诵读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147964_comment'></div>当是时，天下无言古者，野夫复以其幼，而莫有与同其好者焉，但朝暮不释于手，日渐自解之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147964_comment'></div>先大夫见其酷嗜此书，任其所为，亦不责可不可于时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147964_comment'></div>迨年几冠，先大夫以称讳，野夫深得其韩文之要妙，下笔将学其为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147964_comment'></div>诸父有于故里浮屠复浴室者，令野夫为记以试之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147964_comment'></div>野夫时卧疾中，授其言期望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147964_comment'></div>一旦，徵笺墨于病榻，出辞以作之，文无点窜而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147964_comment'></div>家人以为异事，遂腾闻于外之好事者，咸曰：「不可当矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147964_comment'></div>复有怒而笑之者曰：「痴妄儿」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147964_comment'></div>言将我独复其古，家何恣容乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147964_comment'></div>聒聒然大遍于人口矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147964_comment'></div>诸父兄闻之，惧其实不誉于时也，诫以从俗为急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147964_comment'></div>野夫略不动意，益坚古心，惟谈孔、孟、荀、扬、王、韩以为企迹，咸以为得狂疾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147964_comment'></div>后日有制作出于时，众或有下之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147964_comment'></div>乾德戊辰中，遂著《东郊书》百篇，大以机谲为尚，功将馀半，一旦悉出焚之，曰：「先师所不许者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147964_comment'></div>吾本习经耳，反杂家流乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147964_comment'></div>众闻之，益谓不可测度矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147964_comment'></div>厚以化俗为意焉，凡所与往还者，悉归其指诏，亦以为轲、雄之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147964_comment'></div>捧书请益者咸云：「韩之下二百年，今有子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147964_comment'></div>野夫每报之曰：「不敢避是，愿尽力焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子无害其谦之光乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「当仁而不让者，正在此矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147964_comment'></div>或问退之、子厚优劣，野夫曰：「文近而道不同」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147964_comment'></div>或人不谕，野夫曰：「吾祖多释氏，于以不迨韩也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147964_comment'></div>开宝初，又著《东郊野史传》九十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子何以作《野史」》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「野夫之所职也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「何谓《野史」》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「在其国史之外不书者，吾书为《野史》也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子于司马氏、班氏、范氏三家何如也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「司马氏疏略而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/237/Comments/1")'>该辩</span>，泛乱而宏远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147964_comment'></div>班氏辞雅而典正，奇简而采摘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147964_comment'></div>下乎范氏，不迨二家也，多俗气矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147964_comment'></div>吾之所述，居二家之良者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「将何用乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「用之，即有用于世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147964_comment'></div>否，虽先师之书，为长物耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147964_comment'></div>用不用在于世，吾何知哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147964_comment'></div>野夫以古之人不能究天地之真，海之容纳，经之所出，乃作《天辨》、《海说》、《经解》三篇，大能摭其事而證其非，昔贤之所不能及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147964_comment'></div>以而所著文章与韩渐异，取六经以为式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子何始尚而今弃之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「孟、荀、扬、韩，圣人之徒也，将升先师之堂，入乎室，必由之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147964_comment'></div>未能者，或取一家以往，可及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147964_comment'></div>吾以是耳，汝辈有能如吾，可至矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147964_comment'></div>野夫时年始二十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147964_comment'></div>后二年，别立传以书焉，号曰补亡先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147964_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_101_1147964'>论曰：东郊野夫，谓其肩斯，乐古道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147964_comment'></div>谓其绍斯，尚祖德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1147964_comment'></div>退之大于子厚，故以名焉，子厚次之，故以字焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1147964_comment'></div>复以其同时而出，同道而行，今取之偕，信得其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1147964_comment'></div>观其文章行事，烈烈然统二公也，不为过矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_105_1147964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年八月</a>　送高诜赴举，有文。作品：《送高诜赴举序》<div id='poem_1147935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送高铣赴举序</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147935")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147935'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147935'>柳子自谓得圣人之道，好闻人勤其心而专其学者，求其进而安其至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147935_comment'></div>尝曰：时之将幸也，吾道行之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147935_comment'></div>时之不幸也，吾道去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147935_comment'></div>在于天耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147935_comment'></div>在于人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147935_comment'></div>若果在于天，岂不好时之长幸耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147935_comment'></div>如不好，天其否而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147935_comment'></div>吾将谓不在于天而在于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147935_comment'></div>苟君天下者有德也，行吾道者用之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147935_comment'></div>君天下者无德也，则我先师夫子，昔生周末也，何尝能用之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147935_comment'></div>由将用之，则天下之人皆若七十子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147935_comment'></div>宋因于周礼，取文武之道，则而行之九年，万方毕来，归我太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147935_comment'></div>会八月，柳子病起东郊，来入于魏，得其人言宋之同姓大夫逢掌文衡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147935_comment'></div>柳子知大夫之为人公且直也，天子今能用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147935_comment'></div>又言渤海人铣求试于京尹矣，柳子喜而颂曰：熙熙乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147935_comment'></div>煌煌乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147935_comment'></div>道也将行乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147935_comment'></div>吾也将出乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147935_comment'></div>时也将幸乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147935_comment'></div>子野、叔达、季雅从，语三子曰：「余为天下乐得其良有司也，贤者进而不贤者退矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147935_comment'></div>二三子，汝知之乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147935_comment'></div>渤海高生，斯其贤者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147935_comment'></div>上以得其人，下以得其时，吾将与汝永歌而同归吾之东郊，可无辞乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1147935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年</a>　上书符昭愿。作品：《上符兴州书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（是年符昭愿当在兴州刺史任上。）</span><div id='poem_1147903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147903?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上符兴州书</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147903")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147903_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147903'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147903'>予性甚僻，气甚古，不以细行累其心，走四海间求与知者，竟无一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147903_comment'></div>归来乡里，日益时病，常卧草堂下，自称曰野夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147903_comment'></div>仆实非野夫，盖不能苟与俗流辈拘，以自荡厥意，故是言耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147903_comment'></div>每负酒过市，则市人目以为狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147903_comment'></div>晚适田野中，则农夫诟而相笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147903_comment'></div>是魏人不知其人负不羁之材于世也，仆亦不责之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147903_comment'></div>苟上位之人有干于是也，则仆始自惑于心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147903_comment'></div>故今日望执事之门，书以自言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147903_comment'></div>虽贱为布衣，度执事必无加诸仆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147903_comment'></div>况执事乐善进贤，服仁行义，不以贵富骄物，不以勋烈凌材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147903_comment'></div>且九州为大，兆民是众，咸有斯言，岂独仆也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147903_comment'></div>在其下而不有干焉，则使事去而自伤，时失而自咎也，不远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147903_comment'></div>仆尝中夜不寐，自疚其心，满眦尽湿，卒难自禁，非在乎急于食甘衣鲜，求于官荣誉大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147903_comment'></div>况冬一裘而岁暖，朝一饭而日饱，无亲爱离远之痛，无支体瘠劣之疾，盖以其学成而不为人用，道在而不得时迁，虚劳乎师孔子而友孟轲，齐扬雄而肩韩愈，自念其道即反不如百工贱人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147903_comment'></div>且工有长于一伎，民有高于一艺，则众皆凑其室而求其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147903_comment'></div>夫运斤成风者，匠氏之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147903_comment'></div>发矢中的者，匹夫之能：尚皆获其用而沽其直，衒其技而贾其勇，则谁不欲竞致左右，间以观乎能而快乎心矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147903_comment'></div>即仆也，口诵古圣贤人之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147903_comment'></div>心纪古圣贤人之法，作事于世，为民善恶，反与俗伍，日极诋诃，如是岂不痛心哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147903_comment'></div>然江湖可以自放，林泉可以自娱，复恋恋不能去者，以明天子在上，贤执事在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147903_comment'></div>复而思之，设天与其命，一朝一夕，使主张斯文，教民归于古道，又万一而冀望于心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147903_comment'></div>今执事闻是也，忍不察其言而观其行，惜其人而爱其道哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147903_comment'></div>实惟执事少垂奖待，以慰我区区之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1147903_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年</a>　有文。作品：《赠麴直弹琴序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（时间为举进士前，兹系于此处。）</span><div id='poem_1147931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠曲植弹琴序</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147931")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147931'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147931'>我听子之琴，实闻其声，不能知子琴之音也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147931_comment'></div>独坐永日，泠然不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147931_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147931_comment'></div>我是病于子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147931_comment'></div>子谓我能知其音，将欲宣其心，而达其志也，岂徒然乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147931_comment'></div>为子，我悲矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147931_comment'></div>不幸因子琴之悲而切，自感而自悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147931_comment'></div>子果能为我而听其言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147931_comment'></div>子之琴，有似于我之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147931_comment'></div>力学十馀年，非古圣贤之所为用心者不敢安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147931_comment'></div>于是学成而业精，行修而德广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147931_comment'></div>希于古之知己者，不可从而见也，徒勤勤而至于今矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147931_comment'></div>尤于人不我知，诚之而莫所遂其求也，甘自放于东郊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147931_comment'></div>听子之琴，感我之悲也，亦将自尤而自责矣，又何外尤于他人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147931_comment'></div>始自求于人，今知己之为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147931_comment'></div>弃俗尚而专古者，诚非乐于人而取其责者也，独宜其自知而自乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147931_comment'></div>用是而得与子言乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147931_comment'></div>子以琴之能见于我也，将谓我能识其音而辨其功矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147931_comment'></div>我岂果能专为子识其音而辨其功乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147931_comment'></div>易子之愿也，我亦如是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147931_comment'></div>我听子之琴，尚不能识其音而辨其功矣，人岂反能观我之文也，而能为我行其言而尽其道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147931_comment'></div>故知人不我知者，亦无尤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147931_comment'></div>与子务于古者也，知之者不足取于外也，诚乎己而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147931_comment'></div>子闻此之言，固亦信我之感而悲，不为妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147931_comment'></div>子试为我而思之，将见子亦呜呜而不禁矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1147931_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年</a>　为韩昌黎文集作序。作品：《昌黎集后序》<div id='poem_1147938' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147938' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147938?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昌黎集后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（969年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147938")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147938_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147938'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147938'>世谓先生得圣人之道，惜乎不能著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147938_comment'></div>兹为先生之少也，当时之人，亦有是语焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147938_comment'></div>余读先生之文，自年十七至于今，凡七年，日夜不离于手，始得其十之一二者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147938_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147938_comment'></div>先生之时，文章盛于古矣，犹有言也以过于先生，况下先生之后，至于今乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147938_comment'></div>是谓世不知于先生者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147938_comment'></div>夫子之于经书，在《易》则赞焉，在《诗》《书》则删焉，在《礼》《乐》则定焉，在《春秋》则约史而修焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147938_comment'></div>在《经》则因参也而语焉，非夫子特然而为也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147938_comment'></div>在《语》则弟子记其言，纪焉，亦非夫子自作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147938_comment'></div>圣人不以好广于辞而为事也，在乎化天下，传来世，用道德而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147938_comment'></div>若以辞广而为事也，则百子之纷然竞起异说，皆可先于夫子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147938_comment'></div>虽孟子之为书，能尊于夫子者，当在乱世也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147938_comment'></div>扬子云作《太玄》《法言》，亦当王莽之时也，其要在于发圣人之道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147938_comment'></div>自下主于先生，圣人之经籍虽皆残缺，其道犹备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147938_comment'></div>先生于时作文章，讽颂规戒，答论问说，淳然一归于夫子之旨而言之，过于孟子与扬子云远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147938_comment'></div>先生之于为文，有善者益而成之，有恶者化而革之，各婉其旨，使无勃然而生于乱者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147938_comment'></div>是与章句之徒一贯而可言耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147938_comment'></div>且孟子与扬子云不能行圣人之道于时，授圣人之言于人，所以作书而说焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147938_comment'></div>观先生之文诗，皆用于世者也，与《尚书》之号令，《春秋》之褒贬，大《易》之通变，《诗》之风赋，《礼》《乐》之沿袭，《经》之教授，《语》之训导，酌于先生之心，与夫子之旨无有异趣者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147938_comment'></div>先生之于圣人之道，在于是而已矣，何必著书而后始为然也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147938_comment'></div>有其道而无其人，吾所以悲也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147938_comment'></div>有其人而人不知其道，益吾所以悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147938_comment'></div>若先生者，不有人不知其道者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147938_comment'></div>吾谓世不知于先生也，岂为诬言也哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1147938_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年</a>　有文。作品：《天辩》（早佚）《海说》（今存）《经解》（早佚）<div id='poem_1147947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147947?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海说</a><span class='authorDate'>（969年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147947")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147947'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147947'>夏禹理水，东入于海，百川会流，混波而注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147947_comment'></div>能纳是水者，谓乎处下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147947_comment'></div>虽处下也，且水注其内，自古至今，无暂息焉，固有盈而溢之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147947_comment'></div>既不闻有盈而溢之，其水是归何地也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147947_comment'></div>夏禹既能理之，必能知之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147947_comment'></div>所以不言者，阴阳运化之道，自然往复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147947_comment'></div>历代言之者多矣，皆不究其本，讹乱其辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147947_comment'></div>或言纳于尾闾矣，或言注于大荒之中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147947_comment'></div>其馀言者，不复正其所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147947_comment'></div>且言尾闾者，是羿射落之日也，落之为石，其大千里，炎炽其质，故能渗纳其水焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147947_comment'></div>且言注于大荒之中者，言大荒之中有天台之山，有不勾之山，有融天之山，海水或东入焉，或南入焉，或北入焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147947_comment'></div>以予言之，皆非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147947_comment'></div>言尾闾能渗纳其水者，以其炎炽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147947_comment'></div>且物有燃之于火，炎炽极焉，以水沃之，不过一二，即冰然不复能渗纳水矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147947_comment'></div>且海自古已来，积众之水多矣，若尾闾能渗纳其水，岂至今炎炽乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147947_comment'></div>以海沃之，固亦冰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147947_comment'></div>物之情与人之情岂远哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147947_comment'></div>尾闾茍不冰而能渗纳其水，即必有物于今常燃之矣，未知燃尾闾者用何物耳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147947_comment'></div>予是知尾闾之说虚诞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147947_comment'></div>其言海水入于大荒之中山也，是大荒之山内别有纳水之地，未知其水竟在于何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147947_comment'></div>若有纳水之地，亦与此同海矣，岂此不能纳而彼能纳之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147947_comment'></div>其说亦以屈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147947_comment'></div>予以为天地若人之身，江河若人之血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147947_comment'></div>人身之有血，常会于脑，会而复散，归于四支之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147947_comment'></div>茍会于脑，积而不散，即卒成疾矣，疾成于内，人亦殒其命也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147947_comment'></div>运而不竭，是能动转手足，变易神气，为物之灵也，为命之固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147947_comment'></div>江河于天地之间亦若是耳，流会于海，复入于土，散乎四维，居地之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147947_comment'></div>使地能厚载万物者，以水扶之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147947_comment'></div>且掘地逾于寻丈，则必有泉涌而出矣，以是而言，岂不然乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147947_comment'></div>苟若会流于海，无所散入，则混溢天地，垫溺生聚，安足胜也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147947_comment'></div>是知百川之朝于海，不能纳而涸之也，亦复循环天地之中，东而复西，南北从矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147947_comment'></div>阴阳运化，理在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147947_comment'></div>又天地之气，结为山，融为川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147947_comment'></div>结为山者，古有所定，大小高卑，名数无所改易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147947_comment'></div>融为川者，则流而不止，浩浩奔涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147947_comment'></div>岂融为川者，即往而忘反？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147947_comment'></div>结为山者，凝而能定之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147947_comment'></div>苟结而无定，则曰大其形遍天地矣，岂有九州乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147947_comment'></div>岂有万物乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147947_comment'></div>是水其天地之半，山其天地之半也，今之人民，何其处焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147947_comment'></div>是知结为山者，古今定矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147947_comment'></div>融为川者，古今亦定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147947_comment'></div>又或言海有大鱼曰䲡，身横于海之中，朝出其穴，海乃潮焉，暮入其穴，海亦潮焉，䲡之出入有节，故潮之朝暮有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147947_comment'></div>此之说䲡之出入，能致海有潮之进退也，是其穴与海相侔也，未知海之何地乃能容是穴也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147947_comment'></div>又为虚诞甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147947_comment'></div>予以水者，凝阴之气所成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147947_comment'></div>大凡阴阳之气，皆自下而升乎上，日出而阳盛，日入而阴胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147947_comment'></div>夫旦之有潮，以其阳气发于地中，阴气上散，水以阳逼之，故从阴气以溢，乃朝有潮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147947_comment'></div>夕之有潮，以其阴气发于地中，阳气上散，水以阴扶之，故从阳气以浮，乃暮有潮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147947_comment'></div>此之数说于海者，皆不可闻于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147947_comment'></div>然说于此者，未必彼非而我是，彼虚而我实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147947_comment'></div>以情测之，以理究之，即我之说为当矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147947_comment'></div>虑其好迂怪之徒，泯绝吾言，故著其辞以广于我之徒也。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1147947'></div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1147947_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年</a>　高诜下第，作文赠之。作品：《送高诜下第序》<div id='poem_1147929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送高铣下第序</a><span class='authorDate'>（969年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147929")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147929'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147929'>命之短长悬于天，道之屈伸系乎时，德之尊卑由乎己，名之善恶存乎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147929_comment'></div>所谓悬乎天者，寿与夭也，知其命，而可自信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147929_comment'></div>所谓系乎时者，用与舍也，专其道，而可自任矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147929_comment'></div>所谓由乎己者，吉与凶也，务其德，而可自择矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147929_comment'></div>所谓存乎人者，毁与誉也，慎其名，而可自混矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147929_comment'></div>自信而不惑，自任而不废，自择而不怠，自混而不固者，圣人之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147929_comment'></div>不惑，则乐天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147929_comment'></div>不废，则随时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147929_comment'></div>不怠，则勤己；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147929_comment'></div>不固，则顺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147929_comment'></div>能乐乎天，则无忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147929_comment'></div>能随乎时，则无患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147929_comment'></div>能勤乎己，则无阙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147929_comment'></div>能顺乎人，则无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147929_comment'></div>乐天者以仁，随时者以智，勤己者以信，顺人者以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147929_comment'></div>仁以齐之，能齐之者，岂有虞于命哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147929_comment'></div>是曰无忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147929_comment'></div>智以经之，能经之者，岂有害于道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147929_comment'></div>是曰无患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147929_comment'></div>信以诚之，能诚之者，岂有疑于德哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147929_comment'></div>是曰无阙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147929_comment'></div>礼以待之，能待之者，岂有损于名哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147929_comment'></div>是曰无过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147929_comment'></div>若渤海高生者，备于四者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147929_comment'></div>柳子闻之曰：「高生能以仁乐乎天，命之短长也，信其寿夭，曰『予何忧』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147929_comment'></div>予曰：『固何忧矣，子必寿矣』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147929_comment'></div>又曰：「高生能以智随乎时，道之屈伸也，任其用舍，曰『予何患』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147929_comment'></div>予曰：『固何患矣，子将用矣』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147929_comment'></div>又曰：「高生能以信勤乎己，德之尊卑也，择其吉凶，曰『予何阙』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147929_comment'></div>予曰：『固何阙矣，子本吉矣』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147929_comment'></div>又曰：「高生能以礼顺乎人，名之善恶也，混其毁誉，曰『予何过』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147929_comment'></div>予曰：『固何过矣，子难毁矣』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147929_comment'></div>天若不寿子，则子丧，而吾亦丧矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147929_comment'></div>时若不用子，则子阨，而吾亦阨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147929_comment'></div>由乎己者，内求其实也，自我而专之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147929_comment'></div>存乎人者，外贵其华也，自我而取之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147929_comment'></div>若今有司枉子者，命、道、德、名之末耳，虞子之心不在于是，是亦不足极之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147929_comment'></div>勉乎哉，高生！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147929_comment'></div>天下嚣嚣，其谁知子？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147929_comment'></div>微我，则无此言以告于子矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1147929_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　作《野史》成，补诸经忘篇，号补亡先生。作品：《东郊野史》（已佚）<span class='inlineComment2'>（成书。）</span><div id='poem_1147964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东郊野夫传</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147964")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147964'>东郊野夫，肩愈者，名也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147964_comment'></div>绍先者，字也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147964_comment'></div>不云其族氏者，姓在中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147964_comment'></div>家于魏，居邻其郭之门左，故曰东郊也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147964_comment'></div>从而自号之，故曰野夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子邑处而曰郊，士流而曰野，无乃失乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147964_comment'></div>野夫对曰：「吾以为郊，子以为邑矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147964_comment'></div>吾以为野，子以为士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147964_comment'></div>吾宁知郊不为邑，士不为野，是果能质其名之在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147964_comment'></div>苟不果，吾斯不失矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147964_comment'></div>野夫居于家则称曰东郊，出于旅则称曰魏郊，以别内外之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147964_comment'></div>野夫性浑然，朴而不滞，淳而不昧，柔知其进，刚识其退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147964_comment'></div>推之以前不难其行，揖之于后不忿其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147964_comment'></div>来者虽仇而不拒，去者虽亲而不追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147964_comment'></div>大抵取人之长，弃人之短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147964_comment'></div>利不能诱，祸不能惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147964_comment'></div>晦乎若无心，茫乎若无身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147964_comment'></div>不以天地之大独为大，不以日月之明独为明，风雷不疾其变，岳渎不险其固，人莫之识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147964_comment'></div>与其交者，无可否，无疑忌，贤愚贵贱，视其有分，久与之往还，益见深厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147964_comment'></div>或持其无赖之心者，谓其真若鄙愚人也，即事以欺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147964_comment'></div>复有以一得，便再以其二三而谋从计其利，虽后己或自败，野夫与始亦无暂异，竟不言之，然终未有能出其度内者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147964_comment'></div>父兄有以诲而勉之，野夫哑尔笑而对曰：「小儿辈徒劳耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147964_comment'></div>吾尝捕虎于穴，挟其门以利刃，彼于内虽奋跃万变，奈吾当尔隘之阨乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147964_comment'></div>矧若类之蠢蠢哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147964_comment'></div>或有宾自远方至，即倾产以待之，遽与之宴笑寝处无少间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147964_comment'></div>父兄有曰：「汝胡尔为也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147964_comment'></div>一何太疏易乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147964_comment'></div>殊不察其彼之人为若是，无乃不可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147964_comment'></div>野夫曰：「彼人耳，吾人耳，又何间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147964_comment'></div>且天地之中孰有内外也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147964_comment'></div>四海之人皆我之亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147964_comment'></div>己茍有所分别，虽父母兄弟，果肯不以他心待之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147964_comment'></div>己茍无所间于人，即孰忍间于吾乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147964_comment'></div>父兄以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147964_comment'></div>宾既告返，即解衣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>质钱</span>以赆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147964_comment'></div>或贫饿于时，有若可哀者，虽食，减口以遗，恐恐然犹虑不得与之久济矣，不虞其己之反困也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子居贫贱而务施仁义，司马氏之所讥也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147964_comment'></div>野夫对曰：「吁哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147964_comment'></div>君子计人之急，岂谋己乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147964_comment'></div>当贫贱而能施诸仁义，斯所难也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147964_comment'></div>当贵富而将施之，即孰不为能乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147964_comment'></div>且司马氏盖异其君子者耳，所以著书而多离于夫子之旨焉，或退处士而进奸雄，或先黄老而后六经，盖例若此也，吾所耻耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147964_comment'></div>或有结仇相忿者，野夫曰：「汝来前！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147964_comment'></div>何故深憾乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147964_comment'></div>且汝谋彼以复怨，彼作报以图尔，两祸不泯，循环然将何止也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147964_comment'></div>汝无恨他人之不我善，盖自不能善于人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147964_comment'></div>汝茍周于人，即何有不汝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>丰美</span>乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147964_comment'></div>汝见盗之为行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147964_comment'></div>其为残贼污恶，虽父母亦不能容耳，反有同类而相感者，尚皆殒身拒害，有以甘心为交之终始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147964_comment'></div>盖无他，能感彼心以尽我诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147964_comment'></div>盗之犹若是，矧汝辈皆良民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147964_comment'></div>慎勿若此也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147964_comment'></div>仇闻之者，或相解去焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147964_comment'></div>野夫家苦贫，无继夕之粮，无顺时之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147964_comment'></div>年始十五六，学为章句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147964_comment'></div>越明年，赵先生指以韩文，野夫遂乐得而诵读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147964_comment'></div>当是时，天下无言古者，野夫复以其幼，而莫有与同其好者焉，但朝暮不释于手，日渐自解之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147964_comment'></div>先大夫见其酷嗜此书，任其所为，亦不责可不可于时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147964_comment'></div>迨年几冠，先大夫以称讳，野夫深得其韩文之要妙，下笔将学其为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147964_comment'></div>诸父有于故里浮屠复浴室者，令野夫为记以试之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147964_comment'></div>野夫时卧疾中，授其言期望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147964_comment'></div>一旦，徵笺墨于病榻，出辞以作之，文无点窜而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147964_comment'></div>家人以为异事，遂腾闻于外之好事者，咸曰：「不可当矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147964_comment'></div>复有怒而笑之者曰：「痴妄儿」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147964_comment'></div>言将我独复其古，家何恣容乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147964_comment'></div>聒聒然大遍于人口矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147964_comment'></div>诸父兄闻之，惧其实不誉于时也，诫以从俗为急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147964_comment'></div>野夫略不动意，益坚古心，惟谈孔、孟、荀、扬、王、韩以为企迹，咸以为得狂疾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147964_comment'></div>后日有制作出于时，众或有下之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147964_comment'></div>乾德戊辰中，遂著《东郊书》百篇，大以机谲为尚，功将馀半，一旦悉出焚之，曰：「先师所不许者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147964_comment'></div>吾本习经耳，反杂家流乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147964_comment'></div>众闻之，益谓不可测度矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147964_comment'></div>厚以化俗为意焉，凡所与往还者，悉归其指诏，亦以为轲、雄之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147964_comment'></div>捧书请益者咸云：「韩之下二百年，今有子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147964_comment'></div>野夫每报之曰：「不敢避是，愿尽力焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子无害其谦之光乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「当仁而不让者，正在此矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147964_comment'></div>或问退之、子厚优劣，野夫曰：「文近而道不同」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147964_comment'></div>或人不谕，野夫曰：「吾祖多释氏，于以不迨韩也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147964_comment'></div>开宝初，又著《东郊野史传》九十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子何以作《野史」》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「野夫之所职也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「何谓《野史」》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「在其国史之外不书者，吾书为《野史》也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子于司马氏、班氏、范氏三家何如也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「司马氏疏略而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/237/Comments/1")'>该辩</span>，泛乱而宏远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147964_comment'></div>班氏辞雅而典正，奇简而采摘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147964_comment'></div>下乎范氏，不迨二家也，多俗气矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147964_comment'></div>吾之所述，居二家之良者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「将何用乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「用之，即有用于世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147964_comment'></div>否，虽先师之书，为长物耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147964_comment'></div>用不用在于世，吾何知哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147964_comment'></div>野夫以古之人不能究天地之真，海之容纳，经之所出，乃作《天辨》、《海说》、《经解》三篇，大能摭其事而證其非，昔贤之所不能及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147964_comment'></div>以而所著文章与韩渐异，取六经以为式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子何始尚而今弃之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「孟、荀、扬、韩，圣人之徒也，将升先师之堂，入乎室，必由之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147964_comment'></div>未能者，或取一家以往，可及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147964_comment'></div>吾以是耳，汝辈有能如吾，可至矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147964_comment'></div>野夫时年始二十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147964_comment'></div>后二年，别立传以书焉，号曰补亡先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147964_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_101_1147964'>论曰：东郊野夫，谓其肩斯，乐古道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147964_comment'></div>谓其绍斯，尚祖德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1147964_comment'></div>退之大于子厚，故以名焉，子厚次之，故以字焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1147964_comment'></div>复以其同时而出，同道而行，今取之偕，信得其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1147964_comment'></div>观其文章行事，烈烈然统二公也，不为过矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_105_1147964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　改名开，字仲涂，著书。作品：《名解》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　上书王祜。作品：《上大名府王学士书》<div id='poem_1147891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上大名府王祜学士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147891")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147891'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147891'>开再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147891_comment'></div>人之生，有幸与不幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147891_comment'></div>幸者自知，而不幸者谓人莫之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147891_comment'></div>己亦莫之知也，蠢然徒若类而已矣：或出夷狄之中，生不识其礼义，死不知其丧祭，不幸也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147891_comment'></div>或在中国，生不成人而夭，或聋，或瞽，或瘖，或痼，或狂，或愚，皆疾之废也，不幸也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147891_comment'></div>或生当乱世，战伐交兴，相之以贼杀，拘之以俘虏，旦不安其游，夜不宁其居，不幸也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147891_comment'></div>或生困于贫饿，隶人之驱役，受人之制限，贱若于犬马，茍乎衣食者，不幸也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147891_comment'></div>或生为兵，习于弓矢之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147891_comment'></div>生为农，勤于耒耜之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147891_comment'></div>生为工，力于刀斤之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147891_comment'></div>生为贾，务于衡斛之任：唯乎自足者，不幸也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147891_comment'></div>或生溺为老、佛之徒，淫于诞妄之说；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147891_comment'></div>生处乎典吏之职，掌于责罚之繁者，不幸也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147891_comment'></div>是故君子笃道而育德，怀仁而合义，恶夫不幸者也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147891_comment'></div>自古圣人贤士，无不惜乎此矣，生而幸者，少其人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147891_comment'></div>或曰：「子谓是不幸者，谓乎莫若己之皆儒者为幸也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147891_comment'></div>曰：旨哉，吾子之问！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147891_comment'></div>儒者也幸乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147891_comment'></div>幸乎不也已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147891_comment'></div>人之不幸由乎天，身之不幸由乎己，己之者甚乎天之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147891_comment'></div>茍有外其貌而内其情，于儒何幸哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147891_comment'></div>言不忠，行不信，事君不能尽其节，与朋友不能交以义，父母在不能奉其诚，居乡党不能与仁者处，见善不能致而学以及之，闻利喜而趋，耻贫贱而弃，附势而媚容者，虽于身为儒，而曰幸乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147891_comment'></div>其君子观之，不幸也欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147891_comment'></div>存为识者之笑，没为后人之辱，甚乎前之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147891_comment'></div>开窃自念，幸而不生于夷狄之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147891_comment'></div>自五岁而读书，以至于此，凡十九年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147891_comment'></div>当时便诵执事之文章，与夫圣人之言杂而记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147891_comment'></div>敢望今日亲逢执事于是邦哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147891_comment'></div>苟或夭死而疾病，明天子不出而四海乱，堕于执御之中，废先人之业，杂为贱类，纵今逢执事于是邦也，何能进于执事之门哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147891_comment'></div>斯非其幸者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147891_comment'></div>又开粗识古人之事，不敢违道以就其志，诳时以安其身，茍行戾而进于执事之门，亦负惭而自愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147891_comment'></div>开颇有自知其幸也，敢请见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147891_comment'></div>执事倘不罪而宽容之，成乎开之大幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147891_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1147891_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　再上书王祜，求其荐举以应进士试。作品：《上王学士第二书》<div id='poem_1147892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上王学士第二书</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147892")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147892'>开再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147892_comment'></div>先达者，处乎上以待士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147892_comment'></div>后进者，居于下以求知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147892_comment'></div>譬之登高山立其梯焉，前者苟隮而绝其梯，则未隮者无由而来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147892_comment'></div>前若思而自念曰：吾或未得隮于斯，梯忽时而绝，则吾虽趫然迅于猿，翩然利于鸿，则亦莫致是之登其上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147892_comment'></div>所以为上者必资于下，为下者必依于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147892_comment'></div>上茍不容其下，则上之功名无以大，禄位无以尊，独行而无从，独唱而无和矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147892_comment'></div>下茍不从其上，则下之事业无以伸，力行无以施，自为而无朋，自缄而无门矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147892_comment'></div>如此则不惟上下之相失，噫，将见其国亦不得于治，民亦不得于安也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147892_comment'></div>国与民亡其治与安，则礼乐刑政无能措手足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147892_comment'></div>夏、商、周之世，常举其士也，所以王道成而风俗平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147892_comment'></div>秦、汉、魏、晋取士者，或亡或存，故不迨于三代也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147892_comment'></div>夫士之贤愚混，不可不用择其良者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147892_comment'></div>前代之衰乱者，非不取士也，取不以其贤者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147892_comment'></div>君、宰相之下，立百辟庶尹，非徒奉其职而从于政，亦要知其士者，取而致于国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147892_comment'></div>我国家四海今治者，盖得执事者之在于位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147892_comment'></div>执事之心，固常在于取士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147892_comment'></div>当今取士之道，独有礼部焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147892_comment'></div>每岁秋八月，士由乡县而举于州郡，由州郡而贡于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147892_comment'></div>有司试其艺能，择其行义，得中者，后进名于天子，始得为仕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147892_comment'></div>然士之虽有贤能，由乡县而得闻于州郡者，由州郡而得闻于有司者，万少其一二矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147892_comment'></div>况其无贤与能，窃是虚器之人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147892_comment'></div>况其不由乡县州郡而直得闻于执事乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147892_comment'></div>执事之来也，荣矣父母之邦矣，临其下也不以私，御其众也不以党，可与进而进之，不可者否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147892_comment'></div>士咸谓执事于乡里必多乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147892_comment'></div>开曰：君子之心与天道，小人莫能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147892_comment'></div>执事岂以乡里为情哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147892_comment'></div>将以天下为情，于民而与国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147892_comment'></div>千里不足私也，数夫不足党也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147892_comment'></div>接其士者，达于上下相由之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147892_comment'></div>厚与不厚者，取于贤与愚之分异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147892_comment'></div>有之将以济其道，亡之将以顺其物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147892_comment'></div>天可仰而不可升，君子可近而不可亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147892_comment'></div>于士广纳而详择，备求而偏任，执事之所以待于下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147892_comment'></div>开行修而人不誉，辞成而众不解，块然独处，出无与交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147892_comment'></div>亦将由乎乡县而举州郡，岂敢遂望贡于有司乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147892_comment'></div>自度取舍不识向背，材于时而若无用，器于道而如有合，莫知其己之贤且愚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147892_comment'></div>幸逢执事之来，故有望于执事矣，是以三投刺而一奉书，先斋沐而后请见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147892_comment'></div>执事果不罪而与之进退揖让，俯仰周旋，使得尽其仪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147892_comment'></div>执事之若此者，固无失也，盖以接其士而欲求其贤，以致于国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147892_comment'></div>开之幸者则过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147892_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147892_comment'></div>本将由乡县州郡而贡有司，茍得贡于有司，而敢遽望于有司之知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147892_comment'></div>今者不由乡县州郡，而亟得拜见于执事，执事复加之褒扬之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147892_comment'></div>开未知从何而便至于此也，宜何以报执事耳，姑进其言而谢焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147892_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1147892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　再上书王祜，批评当时文风，论道与文之关系。作品：《第三书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　代长兄上书王祜，求知以应举。作品：《代长兄闵上王舍人书》<div id='poem_1147902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代长兄闵上王舍人书</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147902")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147902'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147902'>月日，姓名，上书执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147902_comment'></div>某性识钝劣，惟通经属义而已，然于时事，万亦识其一焉，故知执事乃文章之主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147902_comment'></div>后进于儒者困是道而不能兴，苟得进于左右，间若哀怜而顾悯之，则何复患乎久而穷矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147902_comment'></div>某益念于此，晨夜勿废，非以文也，是难干于执事者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147902_comment'></div>某又不晓于文章，诚将进而莫能进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147902_comment'></div>欲求人而假手之，则有闻于执事者，不可外私于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147902_comment'></div>以此，经时涉日，展转未就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147902_comment'></div>遂以报于小弟，使叙其志，致于文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147902_comment'></div>小弟拒而复不可曰：「兄少乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147902_comment'></div>欲进于执事者，卜恩焉，非艺专而学至，材丰而智深，则孰敢望其门墙而前矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147902_comment'></div>且执事者之有文章也，横天地，冠古今，非司马相如、扬雄之徒，则罔能出于下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147902_comment'></div>自以是薄恶，而何堪写之为辞以干乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147902_comment'></div>如此，将乞怜而反得其责矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147902_comment'></div>不若直其事而质其言，告于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147902_comment'></div>曰：某年十三时，父命授《尚书》于胶东胡生，日诵千百言，兼通大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147902_comment'></div>后二年，又授大《易》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147902_comment'></div>其业之习也，若始之于《书》，虽夜寝而朝食，未尝默口，精之为至，不敢自负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147902_comment'></div>逮年十七，求贡有司，一试而五登于场，越时辈，虽不能中，辄亦无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147902_comment'></div>明年，又贡焉，加一于初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147902_comment'></div>同进者乃相忘而为仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147902_comment'></div>自后岁举于有司，两登名而天子退之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147902_comment'></div>自知命也，时也，不敢恨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147902_comment'></div>二十有五，丁父忧，在家居丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147902_comment'></div>后三年，复求贡焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147902_comment'></div>时遇执事主文衡而综其任，实志于执事也，将能振乎某之困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147902_comment'></div>又不果愿，见退于执事之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147902_comment'></div>某当时颇自悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147902_comment'></div>噫，是己之不专于艺耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147902_comment'></div>是己之拙趋于时耶，是己之失谋于人耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147902_comment'></div>何至于此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147902_comment'></div>去年又进焉，亦见黜于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147902_comment'></div>退而自为，终无所成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147902_comment'></div>七上而七失之，年已三十矣，欲弃之而休，甘伏于圣明之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147902_comment'></div>今年秋，遇执事假政是邦，振养罢危，某复思而喜，将有幸于执事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147902_comment'></div>于古人始立之年，亦未为过，故昨与众而求举焉，未知斯之进也，复何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147902_comment'></div>呜呼，将言之而先泣矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147902_comment'></div>家已贫矣，亲将老矣，身甚长矣，禄由远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147902_comment'></div>天乎，天乎，何罪而是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147902_comment'></div>若此，执事茍不加怜焉，某从何门而望赐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147902_comment'></div>所以冀执事者，亦非诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147902_comment'></div>某为儿时，知执事之声名，诵执事之文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147902_comment'></div>当时远近之言咸曰：『执事终大矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147902_comment'></div>及乎稍长，识执事之形容，执事克已登位于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147902_comment'></div>当时咸曰：『执事虽用而未贵也，斯将入制阁而典文闱，阶乎上也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147902_comment'></div>近年随贡，果当执事选试之内，某虽不见取于执事，人谓执事之升者，实为得贤，咸曰：『执事亦未矣，天子必重寄矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147902_comment'></div>今果理河朔之大邦，化千里而成风，某幸在贡士之流，辱执事之抡举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147902_comment'></div>众复有言，咸曰：『执事必相天下矣，而后展伊周之大谋，振尧禹之德音，万物生植，期荷厥恩』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147902_comment'></div>某从而思之，自念身世，生当执事之同时，幼知执事之圣贤，长见执事之荣泰，近在执事之选试，今受执事之举送，幸为大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147902_comment'></div>执事将必为相矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147902_comment'></div>以乎舆言数四，咸克无虚，故知众人之辞，所果非枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147902_comment'></div>某若冀执事为相之日，期以望恩，时虽不晚，某实免于穷阨也晚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147902_comment'></div>今当执事贡名群士，茍垂怜而振拔之，使有得成，即执事为相之日，移恩在此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147902_comment'></div>兄但志之是言，闻于执事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147902_comment'></div>于执事者茍垂听而不罪之，又何必用于文以干乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147902_comment'></div>某欣然不知所以为之也，直写上献执事，倘三四读而不倦，虽加责，某亦为恩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147902_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1147902_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　竭尽家资为一士人襄葬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年</a>　于东郊教授门徒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年冬</a>　代臧丙作李侯墓志铭。作品：《宋故和州团练使李侯墓志铭》<div id='poem_1147980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147980?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故和州团练使李侯墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（代梦寿作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（971年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147980")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147980'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147980'>惟王建侯，宁邦国，曰：「咨！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147980_comment'></div>尔守节，尔之良，予其耿乃休光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147980_comment'></div>尔之紊，乃成绩颠陨，其追弗庸克自及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147980_comment'></div>予将其试汝，汝侯于乃单」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147980_comment'></div>单惟政有成，「汝其迁于济」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147980_comment'></div>济既五年，始来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147980_comment'></div>曰：「西北，晋奸也，汝居辽以捍之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147980_comment'></div>久弗易厥初民，兵且完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147980_comment'></div>曰：「东南，吴臣也，汝徙和以接之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147980_comment'></div>逮明年，侯死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147980_comment'></div>有仲曰钧，归侯于济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147980_comment'></div>冬，定葬于西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147980_comment'></div>客有志且铭之者，曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1147980'>晋阳李氏者，侯之姓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147980_comment'></div>曰守节而得臣者，侯之名且字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147980_comment'></div>太尉赠封曰植者，侯之曾祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147980_comment'></div>太师赠封曰益者，侯之王父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147980_comment'></div>滑、相、潞三节度曰筠者，侯之先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147980_comment'></div>东头供奉而迨皇城使者，侯之四命而职于内也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147980_comment'></div>始于单而讫于和曰团练使者，侯之四封而牧于外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147980_comment'></div>起仕于周而暨我宋者，侯之历两朝而臣三帝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147980_comment'></div>十五年学于家，而十八年位于世者，侯之寿三十有三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147980_comment'></div>岁辛未而春戊辰者，侯之薨曰开宝四年二月二日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147980_comment'></div>冬季庚寅而襄事者，侯之于是岁而封于墓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147980_comment'></div>二季掌后而主丧者，侯之无子男而有女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147980_comment'></div>哭室而奠帷者，侯之妻曰符氏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147980_comment'></div>某州某县某里者，侯之先茔，今从葬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147980_comment'></div>摭辞而书石者，侯之馆客臧丙梦寿也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1147980_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年冬</a>　答臧丙三书，全面阐述道统论。作品：《答臧丙》三书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（以生而得“圣人之道”及“宋之夫子”自许。）</span><div id='poem_1147901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答臧丙第三书</a><span class='authorDate'>（971年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147901")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147901'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147901'>孰谓吾子不仁，吾不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147901_comment'></div>顺于言而强于道，全于力而公于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147901_comment'></div>尊我之诚，能尽于此诚之尊我若是也，则三有其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147901_comment'></div>始言于予曰：「子达于古文矣，升诸圣人之堂，将入乎室也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147901_comment'></div>再言于予曰：「子之文，克肖于古圣人之文也，无以矜伐取谤，则与先师夫子之文并而显之，亦不废矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147901_comment'></div>又言于予曰：「子为宋之夫子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147901_comment'></div>如是也数，斯深矣言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147901_comment'></div>小渐于大，是曰其顺言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147901_comment'></div>义止于古，是曰其强道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147901_comment'></div>晦用于明，是曰其全力也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147901_comment'></div>诚推于贤，是曰其公人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147901_comment'></div>如谓吾子之不仁，是吾不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147901_comment'></div>予不材德，无尽在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147901_comment'></div>苟虚其己而授其言，则使二三子鸣其鼓而攻于我，我岂能远其二三子也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147901_comment'></div>若其吾子之言有可疑也，则我将复之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147901_comment'></div>我之言曰：「圣人之道果在于我矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147901_comment'></div>吾子惑之，曰：「圣人之道其果在乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147901_comment'></div>其果不在乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147901_comment'></div>夫圣人之道其果不在于我也，则我之述作也，何不取于今，而反取于古也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147901_comment'></div>专于政理之文，是我独得于世而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147901_comment'></div>圣人之道，不谋于己，曲乎其志，从乎其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147901_comment'></div>是能及此，得不谓果在于我矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147901_comment'></div>又若：「夫有学圣人之道者，孰曰圣人之道不在于我也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147901_comment'></div>曰果在于我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147901_comment'></div>夫圣人之道，学而知之者，不得谓之为果也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147901_comment'></div>生而知之者，即得谓之为果也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147901_comment'></div>学而知之者，皆从于师以得之也，得之不能备耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147901_comment'></div>我之所得，不从于师，不自于学，生而好古，长而勤道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147901_comment'></div>况今之人溺于华侈，奔于势利，能求于身，能忘于道，我若从其师以学之，则随而亦化之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147901_comment'></div>若学之曰果也，似有薄于道哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147901_comment'></div>今之学者，依于圣人之道，罕能周而达焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147901_comment'></div>若学之不在圣人之道，则不谓之为学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147901_comment'></div>能学于古圣人之道，则是圣人之道在于今之学者之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147901_comment'></div>我不自于学而得之，是言曰果也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147901_comment'></div>故我之自言得于圣人之道也，不曰从学而来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147901_comment'></div>我若学而得之，不自曰果也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147901_comment'></div>又若：「孔子者，周之大圣人也，生不自知为圣人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147901_comment'></div>夫孔子非不自知为大圣人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147901_comment'></div>若不自知为大圣人也，则又何言曰：「文王既没，文不在兹乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147901_comment'></div>「凤鸟不至，河不出图，吾已矣夫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147901_comment'></div>孔子岂以自知为圣人也，即与当时之人争一国之位，茍存乎养而已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147901_comment'></div>教非不治于世也，当诸侯用伯，明德弗宣，是见阨于衰季也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147901_comment'></div>天茍与其时，孔子岂止位及于一国乎，教治一世乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147901_comment'></div>将使尧舜之垂衣裳也，若其执御耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147901_comment'></div>夫删《诗》《书》，定《礼》《乐》，赞《易》道，修《春秋》，孔子知其道之不行也，故存其教之在其中，乃圣人之事业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147901_comment'></div>后之学者，著一文，撰一书，皆失其正，务尚于辞，未能知其圣人述作之意，又安可出于《诗》、《书》、《礼》《、乐》、大《易》、《春秋》之外欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147901_comment'></div>用其文而行其教也，固然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147901_comment'></div>圣人之道，岂以复能删定赞修于《诗》、《书》、《礼》《、乐》、大《易》、《春秋》，即曰果在于我也，但思行其教而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147901_comment'></div>其为教也，曰道德、仁义、礼乐、刑政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147901_comment'></div>得其时，则执而行之，化于天下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147901_comment'></div>不得其时，则务在昭明于圣人之德音，兴存其书，使不陨坠，何必删定赞修乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147901_comment'></div>况经圣人之手者，文无不备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147901_comment'></div>文茍不备，则不得为世之法也，何足为圣人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147901_comment'></div>夫我言圣人之道果在于我也，即不在删定赞修也，在于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147901_comment'></div>吾子言及于是也，亦失于辞之执耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147901_comment'></div>若吾子以我为宋之夫子也，亦在此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147901_comment'></div>天下之知我能如此也，亦若吾子之谓我矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147901_comment'></div>又何诬于子也，诬于天下也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147901_comment'></div>况圣人之道，不可诬于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147901_comment'></div>茍可诬于人也，则三尺童子坐于儒宫，端弁以处，帅其民以师事之，曰「圣人之道在于斯人也」，如是诬之，可信耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147901_comment'></div>孟轲得圣人之道，岂在复能删定赞修于六经也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147901_comment'></div>扬雄得圣人之道，岂在复能删定赞修于六经也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147901_comment'></div>韩愈得圣人之道，岂在复能删定赞修于六经也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147901_comment'></div>圣人之道，孔子删定赞修之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147901_comment'></div>天生德于孔子，不可偕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147901_comment'></div>孟与扬、韩，或厥绪告微，或厥文告晦，则持而明之，开而辟之，从于孔子之后，各率其辞，各成其书，以佐于六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147901_comment'></div>是曰得圣人之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147901_comment'></div>得之也，三子不在于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147901_comment'></div>况圣人之道不可学也得之者，是曰果也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147901_comment'></div>我窃自比于三子之行事，言之为圣人之道果在于我也，亦不为过矣，亦不在于删定赞修矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147901_comment'></div>又若：「让六经于仁人，不让于不仁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147901_comment'></div>吾子之言诚是也，我虽巧饰其辞，而能拒之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147901_comment'></div>吾子能让于我，虽非其至仁，亦无辱其吾子之让也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147901_comment'></div>让之者不易，纳之者亦难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147901_comment'></div>让失于让则为不知人，纳失于纳则为不度己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147901_comment'></div>能知于人，能度于己，是曰君子也，是曰智者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147901_comment'></div>吾子让之于我不失，我纳之于吾子亦不失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147901_comment'></div>又若「矜伐而取谤」，则敬授命矣，敢不承教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147901_comment'></div>然其间有疑者，辞何已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147901_comment'></div>若谤之取也，无择于君子小人，则君子之与小人道是同也，又何辩其等伦哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147901_comment'></div>若君子观我之文，谤将何取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147901_comment'></div>若小人观我之文，谓我矜伐于今之人，是将兴谤也，则我本非以文矜伐于今之人也，将以文矜伐于古之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147901_comment'></div>矜伐于古之道也，则务将教化于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147901_comment'></div>君子诚之，小人归之，则谤之为渐也，何由而起哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147901_comment'></div>若以文矜伐于今之人也，则不在于古之文也，在于今之所尚者之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147901_comment'></div>轻淫侈靡，张皇虚诈，茍从时欲，求顺己利，是可取谤于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147901_comment'></div>况我之文，不在于此，无求利，无从欲，则小人观之，何得谓我矜伐于今之人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147901_comment'></div>谤不可因而生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147901_comment'></div>若其君子之与小人俱不可取也，固为然耳，复何谈哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147901_comment'></div>若以尧舜之理，则君子之与小人俱被其德，不能兴谤，则谤从何而来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147901_comment'></div>桀纣之代，则君子之与小人俱蒙其恶，是能兴谤，则谤有自而作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147901_comment'></div>夫被尧舜之德也，先君子而后小人，若独有于君子，而无于小人，则不谓之为全德也，何足为兴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147901_comment'></div>蒙桀纣之恶也，亦先君子而后小人，若独有于君子，而无于小人，则不得谓之为全恶也，何足为亡乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147901_comment'></div>君子既被其德，况于小人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147901_comment'></div>君子既蒙其恶，亦况于小人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147901_comment'></div>若以我文之比于君天下者，则有间然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147901_comment'></div>夫君天下者，善恶责于当世，存亡系于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147901_comment'></div>唯文之与道，观其时而行之，观其时而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147901_comment'></div>时之能行即见用当世，时之不行即将贻后代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147901_comment'></div>则又安得与其尧舜、桀纣较其等伦哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147901_comment'></div>孔子之于周也，未闻当其时而能用之，见阨于世，见毁于人，吾子固亦知耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147901_comment'></div>若其畏君子鲜而小人众也，则是君子之道穷，而小人之道胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147901_comment'></div>如此，则君子之不及小人也明矣，况万无此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1147901_comment'></div>岂君子不能成其誉，而小人独能流其谤哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1147901_comment'></div>若茍有是，则君子反为小人之末耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1147901_comment'></div>我之言曰谤取于小人者，盖谓时不能之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1147901_comment'></div>不取乎君子者，谓知其道之有其屈伸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1147901_comment'></div>矧我之能无其可谤于小人哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1147901_comment'></div>时如不能行之，即不在于天下小人之谤，亦不行矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1147901_comment'></div>时如能行之，亦不在二三君子之誉，亦为行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1147901_comment'></div>君子亦不能誉，小人亦不能谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1147901_comment'></div>用与舍，属诸时，誉与谤，属诸命，圣人之达节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1147901_comment'></div>吾子忠告于我，虑于谤，忧于道，我固前言授之耳，亦不敢饰虚辞以拒其教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1147901_comment'></div>若吾子缄其口而默其言，又何轻弃于圣人之道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1147901_comment'></div>辞之可复，我故以答，将谓勉谤而取谤也，则深为失耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1147901_comment'></div>我茍不知吾子之道贤于是也，则谓勉而取谤也，我实小人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1147901_comment'></div>我之前书，吾子再宜思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1147901_comment'></div>思之如有可复，将俟于后命耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1147901_comment'></div>吾子之戒于我，我岂忍违其命也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1147901_comment'></div>重以辞报，义勿能止，非吾子广德渊深，则不足如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1147901_comment'></div>前之所谓三有其说于我也，敬从其言而慎爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1147901_comment'></div>于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1147901_comment'></div>终日论道非不专，专于力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1147901_comment'></div>是非得失，能取于其间者，而今而后，益有望于吾子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1147901_comment'></div>不敢虚也，不敢诬也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_124_1147901_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年冬</a>　作文赠臧丙。作品：《送臧梦寿序》<div id='poem_1147925' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147925' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147925?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送臧梦寿序</a><span class='authorDate'>（971年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147925")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147925_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147925'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147925'>或曰：「君子有求乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147925_comment'></div>于身不可也，于道可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「求益乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147925_comment'></div>求用乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「未达则益，达则用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147925_comment'></div>譬乎造舟于陆，完矣，时济于川矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147925_comment'></div>阙矣，将给请材以备矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「有是乎，君子求之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147925_comment'></div>尧举舜以代天下，舜登而举十六相以理，求之欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「君子求之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147925_comment'></div>舜乎，十六相乎，咸求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147925_comment'></div>时用之，求也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147925_comment'></div>时不用之，固求也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「吾闻舜与十六相，不曰有求，子何曰求乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「德以求之，隐而在下，国有道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147925_comment'></div>孔子旅于七十国，无道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「君子于物，贵恶比」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「如彼质玉也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「质玉处于石，工者采之，以备乎圭璧，玉不求之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147925_comment'></div>如若玉，君子何求乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「砻错以成其器，沽而售之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147925_comment'></div>工视利也，故求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147925_comment'></div>玉以德，工以利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147925_comment'></div>时哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147925_comment'></div>时哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147925_comment'></div>逆顺皆然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147925_comment'></div>君子不求则以德，求则以身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147925_comment'></div>道以由于身者也，身用则用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147925_comment'></div>求而不得者有矣，未有不求而得之者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「吾闻夫臧子欲之辽，有求乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「求也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「求于国若何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「有道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「有道也，何之行而不隐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147925_comment'></div>用之，不求也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147925_comment'></div>不用之，求之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147925_comment'></div>曰：「然亦有矣，趣也异，成也同，及得之一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147925_comment'></div>且辽迩于晋，晋，敌也，恃险以怙凶，违顺以习非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147925_comment'></div>辽以御其冲，晋以防其讨。<div class='inline'
