id='poem_sentence_39_1147925_comment'></div>兵甲之害，曰及民命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147925_comment'></div>臧子于辽守也，将劝义以使革其心，将结信以使断其奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147925_comment'></div>道欲化于辽而来于晋，德乃施诸身而闻诸天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147925_comment'></div>待乎用者也，求之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147925_comment'></div>君子也，有求矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147925_comment'></div>臧子之行也，然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147925_comment'></div>何谓君子无求也哉」！</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1147925_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年冬</a>　作文记高頔授其《昌黎诗》三百首之事。作品：《韩文公双鸟诗解》<div id='poem_1147949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韩文公双鸟诗解</a><span class='authorDate'>（971年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147949")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147949'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147949'>余居东郊，府从事高公独知予，开宝中，授以昌黎诗三百首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147949_comment'></div>开与之会，即赓诵评其尤至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147949_comment'></div>一日，予咨曰：「《双鸟诗》何谓也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147949_comment'></div>公曰：「得无若刺时之政者乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147949_comment'></div>予因而悟之，与公言异，故作辞解之，以编于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147949_comment'></div>高公子奇曰：「双鸟者，当其韩之前后，斯执政人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147949_comment'></div>一以之仕，一以之隐，本异而末同，故曰『落城市』、『集岩幽』，殊以别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147949_comment'></div>下之言，盖以其辨奸诡，比将坏其时也，未知斯孰耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147949_comment'></div>予解曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147949_comment'></div>大凡韩之为心，忧夫道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147949_comment'></div>履行非孔氏者，为夷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147949_comment'></div>忿其正日削，邪日寖，斯以力欲排之，位复不得极其世，权复不得动其俗，唱先于天下，天下从之者寡，背之者多，故垂言以刺之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147949_comment'></div>公曰「何谓也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147949_comment'></div>予曰：「作害于民者，莫大于释、老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147949_comment'></div>释、老俱夷而教殊，故曰双鸟矣，谓其曰此名也，以非仁义、礼乐、父子、君臣之类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147949_comment'></div>其所从来，俱不在于中国，故曰『海外来』也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147949_comment'></div>后渐而至，故曰『飞飞到中州』也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147949_comment'></div>公曰：「若是言之，释之兴也，乃西始矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147949_comment'></div>老之兴也，子何云俱不在于中国乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147949_comment'></div>昔聃著二篇之书，以授其关令，而乃西逝矣，是自此而起耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147949_comment'></div>子如是，无乃误辨韩之旨哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147949_comment'></div>予曰：「然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147949_comment'></div>且聃之昔在中国也，不以左道示民矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147949_comment'></div>暨西入于夷，因化胡以成其教，故欺之以神仙之事，用革其心，而后教乃东来，与昔之书果异耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147949_comment'></div>是非中国之兴也，故韩俱云若是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147949_comment'></div>夫释之为教也，务当民信奉之，架宫崇宇，必处都邑，故曰『一鸟落城市』也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147949_comment'></div>老之为教也，务当自亲其身，收视反听，栖息山林，以求不死，故曰『一鸟集岩幽』也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147949_comment'></div>谓其『不得相伴鸣』也，以其二教之虽来，而未甚明于世，各泯然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147949_comment'></div>言『三千秋』者，以其时久而极言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147949_comment'></div>既未得明其教，其言亦未能大尽于物，故曰各闭其口而衔乎万象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147949_comment'></div>后之正道渐衰，浇妄之风渐盛，故比之『春风』焉，谓其卷地而起，以其举世悉如之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147949_comment'></div>『百鸟皆飘浮』者，众邪以兴也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147949_comment'></div>释、老乃得竞出而扇于民，久益张矣，故曰『两鸟忽相逢，百日鸣不休』也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147949_comment'></div>有耳者聒皆聋，有舌者反自羞，谓其能恢诞而繁极，他莫及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147949_comment'></div>『百舌』，谓百子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147949_comment'></div>从来多善于著书，以乱夫子之道，故曰『旧饶声』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147949_comment'></div>『从此低头』，不能出其上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147949_comment'></div>『得病』，谓其道或世不用之，泯泯遂至死乃休矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147949_comment'></div>世既炽耀其释、老也，说惑于上下之人，极之又不可究其根，无之又不能免其机，遂皆欲舍其生而从矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147949_comment'></div>其间有忿而殊其众者，能大其休声，以愬于上，故曰『雷公告天公』，以假为喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147949_comment'></div>『百物须膏油』者，使世将复其不败于生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147949_comment'></div>故托言云自从其两鸟鸣，而雷光聒亦收矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147949_comment'></div>盖谓其帝王之道不能光行于天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147949_comment'></div>或有哲智之人，将斡运其世务，或诛或殛，以全其变，则惧所以言之有素也，乃停留其造作，而故云『怕嘲咏』矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147949_comment'></div>挑抉其草木，诛求其虫鼠，谓其无所漏脱于幽微也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147949_comment'></div>茍世不息其如此，则咸畏其或生或死，或罪或福，莫知其涯而愁忧矣，故云『不停两鸟鸣，百物皆生愁』也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147949_comment'></div>自此乱，而其时无春秋矣，日月亦莫纪其序矣，大法亦失其九畴矣，周孔之道亦绝灭矣，故曰『周公不为公，孔丘不为丘』也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147949_comment'></div>若此乃释、老之教果遂分焉，虽行于世也，各有拘其时政矣，故曰天公乃怪而各囚于一处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147949_comment'></div>然后世得不全绝其言他道者，乃云百虫百鸟鸣而复啾啾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147949_comment'></div>教之既有其限，不混然，而使民夷也各守其方而省度矣，故曰既别其处而能『闭声省愆尤』也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147949_comment'></div>尚复民之信奉者众，耗于世而害于物，曰亦不知其厚矣，率四海之大，几被其困焉，故曰朝食其龙千，暮食其牛亦千，饮河生尘，而饮海绝其流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147949_comment'></div>其末句云『还当三千秋，更起鸣相酬』者，谓其后必不能终如此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147949_comment'></div>复有其甚惑者，久而见兴也，不限其时而云久也，故以『三千』为言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147949_comment'></div>斯惟韩之在释、老罪，非其他也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147949_comment'></div>公以为如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147949_comment'></div>公曰：「若子之言，韩之诗亦云是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147949_comment'></div>然子能识之，信子于韩氏也，达其玄微也哉」！</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1147949'></div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1147949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年年初</a>　有文。作品：《东郊野夫传》《补亡先生传》<div id='poem_1147964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东郊野夫传</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147964")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147964'>东郊野夫，肩愈者，名也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147964_comment'></div>绍先者，字也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147964_comment'></div>不云其族氏者，姓在中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147964_comment'></div>家于魏，居邻其郭之门左，故曰东郊也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147964_comment'></div>从而自号之，故曰野夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子邑处而曰郊，士流而曰野，无乃失乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147964_comment'></div>野夫对曰：「吾以为郊，子以为邑矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147964_comment'></div>吾以为野，子以为士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147964_comment'></div>吾宁知郊不为邑，士不为野，是果能质其名之在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147964_comment'></div>苟不果，吾斯不失矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147964_comment'></div>野夫居于家则称曰东郊，出于旅则称曰魏郊，以别内外之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147964_comment'></div>野夫性浑然，朴而不滞，淳而不昧，柔知其进，刚识其退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147964_comment'></div>推之以前不难其行，揖之于后不忿其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147964_comment'></div>来者虽仇而不拒，去者虽亲而不追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147964_comment'></div>大抵取人之长，弃人之短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147964_comment'></div>利不能诱，祸不能惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147964_comment'></div>晦乎若无心，茫乎若无身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147964_comment'></div>不以天地之大独为大，不以日月之明独为明，风雷不疾其变，岳渎不险其固，人莫之识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147964_comment'></div>与其交者，无可否，无疑忌，贤愚贵贱，视其有分，久与之往还，益见深厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147964_comment'></div>或持其无赖之心者，谓其真若鄙愚人也，即事以欺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147964_comment'></div>复有以一得，便再以其二三而谋从计其利，虽后己或自败，野夫与始亦无暂异，竟不言之，然终未有能出其度内者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147964_comment'></div>父兄有以诲而勉之，野夫哑尔笑而对曰：「小儿辈徒劳耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147964_comment'></div>吾尝捕虎于穴，挟其门以利刃，彼于内虽奋跃万变，奈吾当尔隘之阨乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147964_comment'></div>矧若类之蠢蠢哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147964_comment'></div>或有宾自远方至，即倾产以待之，遽与之宴笑寝处无少间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147964_comment'></div>父兄有曰：「汝胡尔为也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147964_comment'></div>一何太疏易乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147964_comment'></div>殊不察其彼之人为若是，无乃不可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147964_comment'></div>野夫曰：「彼人耳，吾人耳，又何间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147964_comment'></div>且天地之中孰有内外也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147964_comment'></div>四海之人皆我之亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147964_comment'></div>己茍有所分别，虽父母兄弟，果肯不以他心待之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147964_comment'></div>己茍无所间于人，即孰忍间于吾乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147964_comment'></div>父兄以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147964_comment'></div>宾既告返，即解衣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>质钱</span>以赆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147964_comment'></div>或贫饿于时，有若可哀者，虽食，减口以遗，恐恐然犹虑不得与之久济矣，不虞其己之反困也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子居贫贱而务施仁义，司马氏之所讥也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147964_comment'></div>野夫对曰：「吁哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147964_comment'></div>君子计人之急，岂谋己乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147964_comment'></div>当贫贱而能施诸仁义，斯所难也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147964_comment'></div>当贵富而将施之，即孰不为能乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147964_comment'></div>且司马氏盖异其君子者耳，所以著书而多离于夫子之旨焉，或退处士而进奸雄，或先黄老而后六经，盖例若此也，吾所耻耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147964_comment'></div>或有结仇相忿者，野夫曰：「汝来前！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147964_comment'></div>何故深憾乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147964_comment'></div>且汝谋彼以复怨，彼作报以图尔，两祸不泯，循环然将何止也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147964_comment'></div>汝无恨他人之不我善，盖自不能善于人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147964_comment'></div>汝茍周于人，即何有不汝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>丰美</span>乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147964_comment'></div>汝见盗之为行乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147964_comment'></div>其为残贼污恶，虽父母亦不能容耳，反有同类而相感者，尚皆殒身拒害，有以甘心为交之终始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147964_comment'></div>盖无他，能感彼心以尽我诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147964_comment'></div>盗之犹若是，矧汝辈皆良民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147964_comment'></div>慎勿若此也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147964_comment'></div>仇闻之者，或相解去焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147964_comment'></div>野夫家苦贫，无继夕之粮，无顺时之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147964_comment'></div>年始十五六，学为章句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147964_comment'></div>越明年，赵先生指以韩文，野夫遂乐得而诵读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147964_comment'></div>当是时，天下无言古者，野夫复以其幼，而莫有与同其好者焉，但朝暮不释于手，日渐自解之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147964_comment'></div>先大夫见其酷嗜此书，任其所为，亦不责可不可于时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147964_comment'></div>迨年几冠，先大夫以称讳，野夫深得其韩文之要妙，下笔将学其为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147964_comment'></div>诸父有于故里浮屠复浴室者，令野夫为记以试之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147964_comment'></div>野夫时卧疾中，授其言期望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147964_comment'></div>一旦，徵笺墨于病榻，出辞以作之，文无点窜而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147964_comment'></div>家人以为异事，遂腾闻于外之好事者，咸曰：「不可当矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147964_comment'></div>复有怒而笑之者曰：「痴妄儿」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147964_comment'></div>言将我独复其古，家何恣容乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147964_comment'></div>聒聒然大遍于人口矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147964_comment'></div>诸父兄闻之，惧其实不誉于时也，诫以从俗为急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147964_comment'></div>野夫略不动意，益坚古心，惟谈孔、孟、荀、扬、王、韩以为企迹，咸以为得狂疾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147964_comment'></div>后日有制作出于时，众或有下之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147964_comment'></div>乾德戊辰中，遂著《东郊书》百篇，大以机谲为尚，功将馀半，一旦悉出焚之，曰：「先师所不许者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147964_comment'></div>吾本习经耳，反杂家流乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147964_comment'></div>众闻之，益谓不可测度矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147964_comment'></div>厚以化俗为意焉，凡所与往还者，悉归其指诏，亦以为轲、雄之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147964_comment'></div>捧书请益者咸云：「韩之下二百年，今有子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147964_comment'></div>野夫每报之曰：「不敢避是，愿尽力焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子无害其谦之光乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「当仁而不让者，正在此矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147964_comment'></div>或问退之、子厚优劣，野夫曰：「文近而道不同」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1147964_comment'></div>或人不谕，野夫曰：「吾祖多释氏，于以不迨韩也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1147964_comment'></div>开宝初，又著《东郊野史传》九十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子何以作《野史」》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「野夫之所职也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「何谓《野史」》？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「在其国史之外不书者，吾书为《野史》也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子于司马氏、班氏、范氏三家何如也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「司马氏疏略而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1147964", 1147964, "Clauses/237/Comments/1")'>该辩</span>，泛乱而宏远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1147964_comment'></div>班氏辞雅而典正，奇简而采摘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1147964_comment'></div>下乎范氏，不迨二家也，多俗气矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1147964_comment'></div>吾之所述，居二家之良者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「将何用乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「用之，即有用于世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1147964_comment'></div>否，虽先师之书，为长物耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1147964_comment'></div>用不用在于世，吾何知哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1147964_comment'></div>野夫以古之人不能究天地之真，海之容纳，经之所出，乃作《天辨》、《海说》、《经解》三篇，大能摭其事而證其非，昔贤之所不能及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1147964_comment'></div>以而所著文章与韩渐异，取六经以为式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1147964_comment'></div>或曰：「子何始尚而今弃之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1147964_comment'></div>对曰：「孟、荀、扬、韩，圣人之徒也，将升先师之堂，入乎室，必由之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1147964_comment'></div>未能者，或取一家以往，可及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1147964_comment'></div>吾以是耳，汝辈有能如吾，可至矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1147964_comment'></div>野夫时年始二十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1147964_comment'></div>后二年，别立传以书焉，号曰补亡先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1147964_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_101_1147964'>论曰：东郊野夫，谓其肩斯，乐古道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1147964_comment'></div>谓其绍斯，尚祖德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1147964_comment'></div>退之大于子厚，故以名焉，子厚次之，故以字焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1147964_comment'></div>复以其同时而出，同道而行，今取之偕，信得其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1147964_comment'></div>观其文章行事，烈烈然统二公也，不为过矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_105_1147964_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1147965' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147965' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147965?labeling=true' target='_blank'>补亡先生传</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年年初）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147965")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147965_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147965'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147965'>补亡先生，旧号东郊野夫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147965_comment'></div>既著《野史》，后大探六经之旨，已而有包括扬、孟之心，乐与文中子王仲淹齐其述作，遂易名曰开，字曰仲涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147965_comment'></div>其意谓将开古圣贤之道于时也，将开今人之耳目使聪且明也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147965_comment'></div>必欲开之为其涂矣，使古今由于吾也，故以仲涂字之，表其德焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147965_comment'></div>或曰：「子前之名甚休美者也，何复易之，不若无所改矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147965_comment'></div>先生曰：「名以识其身，义以志其事，从于善而吾恶夫画者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147965_comment'></div>吾既肩且绍矣，斯可已也，所以吾进其力于道，而迁其名于己耳，庶几吾欲达于孔子者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147965_comment'></div>或曰：「古者称已孤不改，若是，无乃不可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147965_comment'></div>先生曰：「执小礼而妨大义，君子不尔为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147965_comment'></div>乃著《名解》以祛其未悟者，众悉以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147965_comment'></div>先生始尽心于《诗》《书》，以精其奥，每当卷叹曰：「呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147965_comment'></div>吾以是识先师之大者也，不幸其有亡逸者哉，吾不得见也，未知圣人之言复加何如耳」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147965_comment'></div>尤于馀经博极其妙，遂各取其亡篇以补之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147965_comment'></div>凡传有义者，即据而作之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147965_comment'></div>无之者，复己出辞义焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147965_comment'></div>故号曰补亡先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147965_comment'></div>先生凡作之书，每执笔出其文，当稿若书他人之辞，其敏速有如此，无续功而成之者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147965_comment'></div>茍一举笔不终其篇，虽十已就其八九，亦弃去不复作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147965_comment'></div>众问之，先生曰：「吾性不喜二三而为之者，方出而或止之，辞意遽纷乱，纵后强继以成之，亦心竟若负病矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147965_comment'></div>或问之曰：「子之《补亡篇》，于古不足当其逸，于今不足益其存，无妄为乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147965_comment'></div>先生对曰：「然纵不能有益于存亡，庶胜乎无心于此者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147965_comment'></div>既而辞义有俱亡不知其可者，虑人之惑，先生即皆先立论以定其是非，用质其旨要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147965_comment'></div>先生常谓人曰：「夫六经者，夫子所著之文章也，与今之人无异耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147965_comment'></div>盖其后之典教不能及之，故大于世矣，吾独视之，与汝异耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147965_comment'></div>先生乃手书九经，悉以细字写之，其卷大者不过满幅之纸，古谓其巾箱之者，亦不过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147965_comment'></div>以而诵之，日尽数万言，未尝废忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147965_comment'></div>有讲《书》以教后学者，先生或诣其精庐，适当至《虞书·尧典篇》，曰「日中星鸟，以正仲春」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147965_comment'></div>说云：「春分之昏，南方朱鸟之星毕见，观之以正仲春之气也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147965_comment'></div>先生乃问曰：「然夫云『日中星鸟，以正仲春』者，是仲春观朱鸟之星，以正其候也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147965_comment'></div>且云朱鸟者，南方之宿，以主于夏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147965_comment'></div>既观其星以正其候，即龙星乃春之星也，春主于东方，可观以正其候也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147965_comment'></div>今何不云是，而反观朱鸟之星，何谓也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147965_comment'></div>说者不能对，惟云传、疏若是，无他解矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147965_comment'></div>先生挥其座者曰：「起前，吾语汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147965_comment'></div>夫岁周其序，春居其始，四星各复其方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147965_comment'></div>圣人南面而坐，以观天下，故春之时，朱鸟之星当其前，故云『观之以正仲春』矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147965_comment'></div>四座无不拜而言曰：「先生真达于经者也，所以于补亡不谬矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147965_comment'></div>先生于诸经若此者，不可遍纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147965_comment'></div>先生又以诸家传解笺注于经者，多未达穷其义理，常曰：「吾他日终悉别为注解矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147965_comment'></div>大以郑氏笺《诗》为不可，曰：「吾见玄之为心，务以异其毛公也，徒欲强己一时之名，非能通先师之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147965_comment'></div>且《诗》之立言，不执其体，几与《易》象同奥，若玄之是笺，皆可削去之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147965_comment'></div>又以《论语集解》阙注者过半，曰：「古之人何若是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147965_comment'></div>吾闻韩文公昔重注之，今吾不得见，吾将下笔，又虑与韩犯，使吾有斯艰也，天乎哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147965_comment'></div>先生每读《中说》，叹曰：「后之夫子续六经矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147965_comment'></div>世故道否，吾家不克有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147965_comment'></div>甚乎，年之始成也，逝矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147965_comment'></div>天适与其时，行之为事业，尧舜不能尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147965_comment'></div>茍不死，天下何有于唐哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147965_comment'></div>先生以房、杜诸子散居厚位，叶佐其主，遇其君不能扬其师之道，大其师之名，乃作书以罪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147965_comment'></div>先生所行事，人咸以为非可与伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147965_comment'></div>范诗有《复古》之什以颂其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147965_comment'></div>以其先生能敦复于古，故赋《复古》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147965_comment'></div>以其能行仲尼之道，故赋《阙里》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147965_comment'></div>以章别当世之人，能作《野史》，故赋《踵孟》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147965_comment'></div>以其能解释子云之书，故赋《先雄》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147965_comment'></div>以其或笔削其韩文之繁者，故赋《删韩》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147965_comment'></div>以其将求太常第，故赋《多文》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147965_comment'></div>以其必首冠于四科，故赋《高第》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147965_comment'></div>以其后天王俾不家食，故赋《出禄》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147965_comment'></div>以其将果得其位，则指南于吾道，故赋《指南》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147965_comment'></div>末以释经终其篇，谓其章明经旨，永休于世用，故赋《释经》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147965_comment'></div>先生见之曰：「范果知我矣，天之未丧斯文哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147965_comment'></div>天之若丧斯文也，则世无范矣，范无是言矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147965_comment'></div>开宝中，先生来京师，遂刻石为记于补亡亭内，以志其己之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147965_comment'></div>后从仕于世而行其道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147965_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1147965'>论曰：孔子没，经籍遭秦之焚毁，几丧以尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147965_comment'></div>后之收拾煨烬之馀者，得至于今用之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147965_comment'></div>其能继孔氏者，轲之下，虽扬雄不敢措一辞，以至亡篇阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147965_comment'></div>而其名具载，设虚位，使历代诸君子徒忿痛而见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147965_comment'></div>故有或作而补之者，夫亦不能过其百一，力盖不足继也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147965_comment'></div>隋之时，王仲淹于河汾间，务继孔子，以续六经，大出于世，实为圣人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147965_comment'></div>是以门弟子佐唐用王霸之道，贞观称理首，永十八君之祚，尚非其董恒辈之曾及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147965_comment'></div>于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147965_comment'></div>知圣人之道者，成圣人之业矣，吾犹不得见王氏之书乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1147965_comment'></div>观夫补亡先生能备其六经之阙也，辞训典正，与孔子之言合而为一，信其难者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1147965_comment'></div>若王氏之续六经，盖自出一家之体裁，比夫《补亡篇》，力少殊耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1147965_comment'></div>所谓后生可畏者，虽经籍尚能补之，矧其馀者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1147965_comment'></div>不可谓代无其人也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1147965_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年闰二月</a>　上窦僖书，求发解以应进士试。作品：《上窦僖察判书》<div id='poem_1147905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上窦僖察判书</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年闰二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147905")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147905'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147905'>后二月五日，开再拜，谨奉书于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147905_comment'></div>今之所谓进士者，天下几百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147905_comment'></div>凡所能中有司之选者，其道有三，非材、非力、非智，即不得从其列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147905_comment'></div>斯三者，能用其一，皆为取名之良者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147905_comment'></div>材者为上，力者为次，智者为下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147905_comment'></div>于三之中，茍复能参用其二者，即誉之与位，劳不失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147905_comment'></div>有能兼是者，由来鲜哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147905_comment'></div>夫所谓材者，文章也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147905_comment'></div>力者，权势也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147905_comment'></div>智者，朋党也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147905_comment'></div>文章之用，固如金石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147905_comment'></div>权势之要，疾如风雷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147905_comment'></div>朋党之附，密如胶漆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147905_comment'></div>士或学深而行广，辞古而道周，昭明足以不昧其光，执确足以能守其节，是来取名也，有司果肯遗其材之异乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147905_comment'></div>士或门崇而地峻，父贵而兄显，荣辱足以擅动于世，上下足以尽归于己，是来取名也，有司果敢拒其力之大乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147905_comment'></div>士或颜茍而心谀，迹勤而言媚，趋竞足以巧结于众，偷贱足以曲屈于气，是来取名也，有司果能免其智之谋乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147905_comment'></div>若是者，果道之有其三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147905_comment'></div>然以材而得之者，有誉而无谤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147905_comment'></div>以力而得之者，有谤而无誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147905_comment'></div>以智而得之者，谤与誉也，俱泯然无所闻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147905_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147905_comment'></div>材以众伏，力以众怒，智以众和，其所以于其己也，亦各从其所以尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147905_comment'></div>能以材之取其名者，其为行也常，故日经久而誉增，业复修而位高，故曰上矣，如金石矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147905_comment'></div>能以力之取其名者，其为行也暴，故始或盛而终衰，事虽成而德败，故曰次矣，如风雷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147905_comment'></div>能以智之取其名者，其为行也安，故时既平而道常进，莫知而退销，故曰下矣，如胶漆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147905_comment'></div>友朋间凡进于有司者，开常以是言告之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147905_comment'></div>其取名之者，彼于得失也，无能逃脱于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147905_comment'></div>或三者之中俱无一也，见其来而私惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147905_comment'></div>开本在魏东郊，著书以教门弟子，愿有终焉之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147905_comment'></div>不幸迩来父兄以家贫，令求禄以养生，交朋以时亨，勉趋仕以专道，故束带冠发，编修简策，欲陪士君子之下，有冀望于名焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147905_comment'></div>退而自度，其己之于时也，正在此常惧者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147905_comment'></div>谓其材也，即文章不合于俗尚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147905_comment'></div>谓其力也，即权势下列于民仵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147905_comment'></div>谓其智也，即朋党绝疏于世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147905_comment'></div>如是求而望得也，可不艰哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147905_comment'></div>或谓子可从人以访诸，用决其得且失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147905_comment'></div>开遂北走是来，愿伏门下，以冀执事之知，进退之间，唯执事之命耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147905_comment'></div>故以是书，敢为贽业之先容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147905_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1147905_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年闰二月十七日</a>　再上窦僖书。作品：《上窦僖察判第二书》<div id='poem_1147906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147906' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147906?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上窦僖察判第二书</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年闰二月十七日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147906")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147906_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147906'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147906'>后二月十七日，开再拜言于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147906_comment'></div>昔楚人有大玉将求厚价以售之者，怀之日久，世莫能识其宝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147906_comment'></div>知秦有公子尚奇货者，来造之，以玉愿纳焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147906_comment'></div>秦公子曰：「吾甚贵子之玉，以吾家苦贫，不足当子之直也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147906_comment'></div>然与吾游者有大富家，可沽之矣，吾为子贾于其人焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147906_comment'></div>楚人从之，富之家果丰其直以取其玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147906_comment'></div>他日命工成器，以出于世，世咸谓非常者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147906_comment'></div>皆曰：「斯璞实楚人有之，有公子能识之，某富之家乃得之，于今所以见贵于时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147906_comment'></div>昔非公子之力也，即楚人虽有，而不得售于世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147906_comment'></div>富家虽存，而不得市其宝矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147906_comment'></div>开窃敢比焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147906_comment'></div>虽非奇能畯博之材，欲求异乎常流者，即开有之矣，于世是所难得其知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147906_comment'></div>闻执事之贤，故远以来，冀执事若秦公子之识而垂力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147906_comment'></div>执事茍未能自以售其人，即执事言于他能贵士者可取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147906_comment'></div>如后日之使开有所称于世，行义或立于一时，文章或垂于万代，众之人必曰柳开之材之能实如是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147906_comment'></div>其所以知者，必曰执事也致其某人，得之出于门下，其功或有是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147906_comment'></div>茍非某执事者，即柳开虽异于人，而安得遂其志乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147906_comment'></div>某之人虽欲其贤，而安得知其人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147906_comment'></div>若是者，与楚人之玉亦无殊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147906_comment'></div>其所以称者，执事必当其首也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147906_comment'></div>此事非其妄言，执事度之，足以信其实与伪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147906_comment'></div>古之时或能举材荐贤者，于今言之，谁不知之，其曰有某士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147906_comment'></div>今亦若古耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147906_comment'></div>其有玩好，间家得一稀见之物，尚贵而惜之，或访其来，则必常称曰某之人遗某，某之人贾某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147906_comment'></div>况其得于士哉，有反不言者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147906_comment'></div>是其知而举之者，甚于取而得之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147906_comment'></div>又其当今之文士才子，虽国家崇异此道，碌碌散满于天下，或有已得名者，或有未得名者，观其徒即繁，求其人即少，若较其杰出者，不过五六人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147906_comment'></div>范师回、李天钧、郭杲之、宋素臣、孙文通、李守之之辈，或文，或才，皆谓众不能及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147906_comment'></div>众称此数君子之中，曰某人者是某之能知其才也，某之能重其文也，某之力与举之也，某之力与推之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147906_comment'></div>且与执事或谈之，岂有异于此言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147906_comment'></div>是其或能力于此数君子者，诚为美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147906_comment'></div>况其此数子之中，受知与恩于执事之门下者过半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147906_comment'></div>其间宋素臣、孙文通是故仆射公之门生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147906_comment'></div>范师回之文行，兄事于执事，非执事知其人，彼何肯如是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147906_comment'></div>李守之，执事拔于孤贱之中，举其才能，使获科第也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147906_comment'></div>若此举材得贤之名，执事之门半天下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147906_comment'></div>执事茍能固其诚，执其义，有所贤，抱所能者，谁不延颈而望，叠迹而来矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147906_comment'></div>开非自尊之论，其与此数君子，亦有一日之长，可容厕其间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147906_comment'></div>敢望执事以一言而见知，以万力而拔举也，不是虚矣，不是二三其求矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147906_comment'></div>执事之心，果肯若前芳而不弃于材，即开之志不误其此来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147906_comment'></div>事蹙时迫，辞旨恳切，馀其面闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147906_comment'></div>死罪死罪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147906_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1147906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>　上书范员外以求知。作品：《与范员外书》<div id='poem_1147896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147896?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与范员外书</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147896")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147896_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147896'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147896'>孟春晦日，东郊柳子言于范侯曰：世之学者，取于今而不取于古，其名问虽显，而事业不著；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147896_comment'></div>世之仕者，专于身而不专于道，故其禄位虽尊，而德义不彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147896_comment'></div>取于今者，是谓趋于时者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147896_comment'></div>专于身者，是谓好于利者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147896_comment'></div>学者以名问为华，而事业为实，茍能于华而不能于实，曰妄于学也，学之下者也，圣人耻之，予亦耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147896_comment'></div>茍能于华而兼能于实，曰通于学也，学之中者也，圣人可之，予亦可之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147896_comment'></div>茍能于实而不能于华，曰达于学也，学之上者也，圣人多之，予亦多之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147896_comment'></div>仕者以禄位为轻，而德义为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147896_comment'></div>茍爱于轻，不爱于重，曰滥于仕也，仕之下者也，圣人恶之，阁下亦恶之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147896_comment'></div>茍爱于轻，而兼爱于重，曰守于仕也，仕之中者也，圣人容之，阁下亦容之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147896_comment'></div>茍爱于重，而不爱于轻，曰强于仕也，仕之上者也，圣人贵之，阁下亦贵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147896_comment'></div>故予多其达于学也，为文常务于教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147896_comment'></div>故阁下贵其强于仕也，为政常务于治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147896_comment'></div>教以仁义为先，治以忠信为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147896_comment'></div>先者，仁以存其诚，义以制其体，务在于其教也，则予不能趋于时，果名问不显，而事业著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147896_comment'></div>本者，忠以事其上，信以临其下，务在于其理也，则阁下不能好于利，果禄位不尊而德义彰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147896_comment'></div>能趋于时，能好于利者，未有取于古而专于道也，是曰小人之徒欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147896_comment'></div>能取于古，能专于道者，未有趋于时而好于利也，是曰君子之徒欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147896_comment'></div>小人不能及君子之事，故其名问显而不永，禄位尊而不固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147896_comment'></div>君子不足取小人之任，故其事业著而益光，德义彰而愈明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147896_comment'></div>今之学者，取小人而弃君子，则予常反于是，是以予也不得不穷为一旅人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147896_comment'></div>今之仕者，亦取小人而弃君子，则阁下亦常反于是，是以阁下不得不阨于一外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147896_comment'></div>予所穷之于身也，何足为穷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147896_comment'></div>若穷之于文也，则是为穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147896_comment'></div>阁下所阨之于位也，何足为穷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147896_comment'></div>若阨之于政也，则是为穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147896_comment'></div>况今君天下者曰圣，宰天下者曰贤，又将见予之身不穷矣，阁下之位不阨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147896_comment'></div>予观阁下之为政也，尽得其专于道而务于治也，不足复言之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147896_comment'></div>阁下观予之为文也，未尽能其古而务于教也，则谨以碑、铭、箴、疏、论等杂共一十五篇，献于左右，间冀阁下知斯言之不佞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147896_comment'></div>惟于愚不肖，与阁下望其等伦，则有悬于贵贱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147896_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1147896_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f9a3af7279e94f5393959ff9d183da0d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f9a3af7279e94f5393959ff9d183da0d");'><span id='f9a3af7279e94f5393959ff9d183da0d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>，38岁</div><div id='f9a3af7279e94f5393959ff9d183da0d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年年初</a>　离润州任，归京。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c1557b14fb284936a44fd9d3cf8a4b53_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c1557b14fb284936a44fd9d3cf8a4b53");'><span id='c1557b14fb284936a44fd9d3cf8a4b53_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>，39岁</div><div id='c1557b14fb284936a44fd9d3cf8a4b53' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年五月</a>　过大名府南行。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title

-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='755690b4a43f49afa22541f16a0dbd41_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("755690b4a43f49afa22541f16a0dbd41");'><span id='755690b4a43f49afa22541f16a0dbd41_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=964&endYear=965')">964-965年</a>，18-19岁</div><div id='755690b4a43f49afa22541f16a0dbd41' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=964&endYear=964')">964年</a>　侍父赴京，父拜监察御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=965&endYear=965')">965年年初</a>　是年父拜泗州通判。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='20c87cc3ff13485da95ef3a35273fa07_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("20c87cc3ff13485da95ef3a35273fa07");'><span id='20c87cc3ff13485da95ef3a35273fa07_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>，26岁</div><div id='20c87cc3ff13485da95ef3a35273fa07' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年夏初</a>　至京师，贽文翰林学士卢多逊，求于开封府发解。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c18a4d9764074e0da824c84a79242940_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c18a4d9764074e0da824c84a79242940");'><span id='c18a4d9764074e0da824c84a79242940_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=973')">972-973年</a>，26-27岁</div><div id='c18a4d9764074e0da824c84a79242940' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年四月十五日</a>　答梁周翰书，自述改今名今字的原因。作品：《答梁拾遗改名书》<div id='poem_1147897' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147897' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147897?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答梁拾遗改名书<span class='inlineComment2'>（周翰，开宝壬申年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（972年四月十五日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147897")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147897_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147897'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147897'>四月十五日，乡贡进士柳开再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147897_comment'></div>始其愚之名肩愈也，甚幼耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147897_comment'></div>其所以志之于文也，有由而来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147897_comment'></div>年十六七时，得赵先生言，指以韩文，遂酷而学之，故慕其古而乃名肩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147897_comment'></div>复以绍先字之，谓将绍其祖而肩其贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147897_comment'></div>愚之所自著《东郊野夫传》者，于《论》言之备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147897_comment'></div>其《传·论》曰：「东郊野夫，谓其肩斯，乐古道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147897_comment'></div>谓其绍斯，尚祖德也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147897_comment'></div>亦所以见小人之所为，尽于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147897_comment'></div>迩自庚午岁，《野史》既绝笔，于东郊取诸经亡篇补之，后自赓其号曰补亡先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147897_comment'></div>去秋八月已来，遂有仕进之心，以干于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147897_comment'></div>故得今以所著文投知于门下，实为之举进士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147897_comment'></div>窃冀于公者，公以言誉之，公以力振之，同于常辈而是念矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147897_comment'></div>不谓公厚待曰：「贤过于韩吏部」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147897_comment'></div>赐书责其不至曰：「若肩于韩而为名，非所然也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147897_comment'></div>以至指摘韩氏之疵，恐累于小人之尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147897_comment'></div>信公于古无与俦者耳，小人谨闻命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147897_comment'></div>然若韩氏之录顺宗、纪淮西、谏佛骨、碑罗池，其文在于今，其事显于古，是非岂能曲于蔽与诬者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147897_comment'></div>凡圣贤之度量大同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147897_comment'></div>唐之时，亦谓韩为轲、雄之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147897_comment'></div>于今亦咸云若是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147897_comment'></div>又其言文之最者，曰元，韩、柳、陆也，是韩亦有道耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147897_comment'></div>李让夷撰录于韩氏，近又以传之者，皆指斥此数事，若方之于公，即俱不足道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147897_comment'></div>昔先师夫子，圣人也，为独立于古今矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147897_comment'></div>马迁氏纪《老聃传》即有他辞，以劣于先师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147897_comment'></div>是亦其复有大于圣人者也，矧其馀为贤者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147897_comment'></div>公之以韩氏未足为可贤也，盖公之大于韩氏矣，亦若李聃之与先师夫子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147897_comment'></div>不其公见之者异于人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147897_comment'></div>得不贵之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147897_comment'></div>若教小人之更其所慕也，即小人本在渐，而不在于久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147897_comment'></div>幼之时，所以名者，在于好尚韩之文，故欲肩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147897_comment'></div>逮今长而成，所以志者，在乎执用先师之道也，故亦将有所易矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147897_comment'></div>是以《补亡先生传》曰：「补亡先生，旧号东郊野夫者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147897_comment'></div>既著《野史》，后复探六经之旨，以而有包括扬、孟之志，乐与文中子王仲淹齐其述作，遂易名曰开，字仲涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147897_comment'></div>其意谓将开古圣贤之道于时也，将开今人之耳目使聪且明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147897_comment'></div>必欲开之为其涂矣，使古今由于吾也，故以仲涂字之，表其德焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147897_comment'></div>斯亦小人之志，不执其名于肩韩氏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147897_comment'></div>《传》又云：「或曰：『子前之名甚休美者也，何复易之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147897_comment'></div>不若无所改矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147897_comment'></div>先生曰：『名以识其身，义以志其事，从于善而吾恶夫画者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147897_comment'></div>吾既肩且绍矣，斯可已也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147897_comment'></div>所以吾进其力于道，而迁其名于己耳，庶几吾欲达于孔子者也』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147897_comment'></div>斯亦小人之志，又周于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147897_comment'></div>小人杂著文中，又有《易名解》，以解其名肩愈，而将易曰开也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147897_comment'></div>公以是观之，小人果何如也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147897_comment'></div>夙昔之心，正符公今之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147897_comment'></div>公谓小人之文，窥六经之奥，正百家之失，廓尧、舜之王涂，张周、孔之至治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147897_comment'></div>管、晏之俦，霸者之佐，未称其小人之所包括也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147897_comment'></div>即倘小人茍实有是，岂果在未名于天朝乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147897_comment'></div>复白：疑之真有耶，无耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147897_comment'></div>望公细而阅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147897_comment'></div>亦前所贡于公之文中有传，名斯在矣，敢承诲命，遽定曰开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147897_comment'></div>旅馆嚣然，文思不生，言无所常道者，急于报谢，勿怪之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147897_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1147897_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年十一月</a>　再次上书卢多逊，乞援引。作品：《上卢学士书》<div id='poem_1147912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147912?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上卢学士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147912")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147912'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147912'>十一月日，乡贡进士柳开再拜，奉书于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147912_comment'></div>开始将求进于有司也，或有告开者曰：「古圣人思欲爱民也深矣，作卜筮以见乎神，存蓍龟以定其器，民有疑于事者，可以占夫利不利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147912_comment'></div>今子将进于有司也，无乃须以谋于此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147912_comment'></div>龟筮从以行之，龟筮违以止之，斯免子于妄进矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147912_comment'></div>开对之曰：「夫人之作事于世也，物或可用之，物或可舍之，蓍龟于何有乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147912_comment'></div>且开读书著文，干进于时，自有上位之君子知夫利不利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147912_comment'></div>必若己不能谋于人，假其蓍龟以告卜之，则吉凶未能胜于贤君子也，开其不若卜于上位之人矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147912_comment'></div>开退而思之，私自言曰：今夫朝廷之贤者，独执事大矣，果将往而卜之，与之进而斯进矣，与之退而斯退矣，是可定于开之利不利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147912_comment'></div>故夏初求先容以登于执事之门，直以恶文干于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147912_comment'></div>洎乎面见执事，果执事不曰汝未可以进矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147912_comment'></div>凡近年举进士者，唯开封解为盛，礼部升而中第者十居其五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147912_comment'></div>所以天下之士群来而求荐焉，争先而冀上焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147912_comment'></div>开实不忍弃之，大望其角胜矣，乃尝拜而有谋于执事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147912_comment'></div>执事当是时，飏言而命开曰：「汝何必须开封解矣，去年李蔚解于郑而成名，有司不遗其材，斯果在于开封乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147912_comment'></div>汝但敩其李蔚耳，无执于内外解也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147912_comment'></div>开退且喜曰：开之进也，知其利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147912_comment'></div>明公赐开之言，如是见成败也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147912_comment'></div>吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147912_comment'></div>向者告开以蓍龟而卜志者，果不能若开之始愿也，如走夷路而获良马焉，指八极而可坐到耳，实不觉气之雄，心之飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147912_comment'></div>迩者遂西入郑郊，果获首荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147912_comment'></div>开是知其进有利于有司矣，岂不尽系于执事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147912_comment'></div>且士之立世而行道，显名而取位者，孰能自用而自荐乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147912_comment'></div>须以上位之人知而必爱其材也，可以遂其求矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147912_comment'></div>设上位之人不能知而爱其材，则虽有仲尼氏之圣之道，亦将困而遑遑焉，不获其志矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147912_comment'></div>自秦汉以来，有名之士登用于民上者，谁不曰某因某而彰于时，某因某而获于位乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147912_comment'></div>今由古也，弗可废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147912_comment'></div>开虽不敏，愿从事于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147912_comment'></div>开受性介僻，与世少合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147912_comment'></div>今虽司贡士，执事不当于任，然望赐于执事也，誓心不迁矣，愿出于执事之门下，开实为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147912_comment'></div>必有后之人言曰：「柳开能有是，名有是，非柳开则执事不举矣，非执事则柳开不往矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147912_comment'></div>茍获与古贤君子齐其休美，后之人果若是而称论之，则开虽朝受赐而夕死可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147912_comment'></div>荷执事之恩，宜将何报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147912_comment'></div>姑致谢而进斯言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147912_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1147912_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=973&endYear=973')">973年</a>　曾贽文知贡举李昉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=973&endYear=973')">973年二月</a>　再上书李昉，为李昉辩谤。作品：《上主司李学士书》<div id='poem_1147908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上主司李学士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（973年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147908")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147908_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147908'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147908'>二月日，乡贡进士柳开再拜，献书于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147908_comment'></div>夫世有君子小人，则有毁誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147908_comment'></div>毁誉茍不以其道，则君子小人是非不为当矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147908_comment'></div>大凡善与不善，各从其类而作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147908_comment'></div>毁之为道，不善者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147908_comment'></div>誉之为道，善者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147908_comment'></div>故君子为善也，多誉人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147908_comment'></div>小人为不善也，多毁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147908_comment'></div>誉人者，乐人之有得；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147908_comment'></div>毁人者，乐人之有失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147908_comment'></div>是以君子与小人相反焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147908_comment'></div>为行茍同于君子，必誉之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147908_comment'></div>既君子以誉之，则小人必毁之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147908_comment'></div>毁之也者何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147908_comment'></div>以其性不合而气使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147908_comment'></div>为行茍同于小人，则小人必不毁之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147908_comment'></div>既小人不毁之，则君子不为誉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147908_comment'></div>君子之不为誉者，以其合于小人而善不可见于时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147908_comment'></div>盖君子之誉者，必为善之徒也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147908_comment'></div>小人之不毁者，必为不善之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147908_comment'></div>是以大君子不纳小人之毁于人者，以此章明其善与不善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147908_comment'></div>且君子誉人之善，小人必为之随而毁者，盖于古即以嫉其道，于今即以争其名，是以古今不能无毁于善者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147908_comment'></div>若君子之下，世无其小人，即誉之下，毁几乎息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147908_comment'></div>有天地来，未见独有君子而绝无其小人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147908_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147908_comment'></div>将奈斯者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147908_comment'></div>必若小人未能世无之，即有誉者，或为其毁而致失也，君子不可不虑于心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147908_comment'></div>开之于今，正在此之忧惧中耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147908_comment'></div>自去年秋应举在京师间，士大夫或以恶文见誉者多矣，度明公之所亦甚知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147908_comment'></div>是以小子行事之间，不复列于此书者，以开所纳文中，有《东郊野夫》及《补亡先生》二传可以观而审之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147908_comment'></div>为人也，誉之声从来既有矣，毁之者果不能无之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147908_comment'></div>窃听近日嚣嚣成风，兴谤之徒十或一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147908_comment'></div>誉开者，斯既君子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147908_comment'></div>毁开者，斯必小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147908_comment'></div>度明公必不以小人之毁，而易君子之誉开也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147908_comment'></div>然自有礼部岁贡士来，岁岁群进于有司也，有材者必有誉，有誉者必有成，既而材斯异，誉斯至，成斯见，未有一人能免其小人之群毁也，故明公之所深察者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147908_comment'></div>开之大王父<span class='inlineComment2'>（讳㻮）</span>唐光化中赵公<span class='inlineComment2'>（讳光逢）</span>司贡士也，实来应举，赵将以榜末处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147908_comment'></div>遽有移书于赵公毁我先君者，赵公始得一书，乃迁其名而进一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147908_comment'></div>以至于前后得谤书二十六通，赵公每得一书而必一进名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147908_comment'></div>是岁也，赵下二十七人，故我先君名止于第二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147908_comment'></div>茍是时书未止于二十六人之毁也，即必冠乎首矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147908_comment'></div>我先君后果作相于唐，而有力扶大难之美，陷乎身，而君子到于今称之，贵赵公特达之能如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147908_comment'></div>开虽不敢望踵于先人，而明公岂肯使赵专美也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147908_comment'></div>况古圣贤人，未有不为小人之毁者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147908_comment'></div>在周，则周公有流言之谤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147908_comment'></div>在鲁，则孔子有桓魋之毁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147908_comment'></div>在齐，则孟轲有臧仓之訾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147908_comment'></div>在汉，则扬雄有投阁之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147908_comment'></div>开之道，学圣贤人而然未臻其极，若其取于小人之毁也，不能免圣贤人之有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147908_comment'></div>在开思之，复甚于古圣贤人之得毁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147908_comment'></div>且周、孔、孟、扬之徒，致其小人之毁也，止以其道耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147908_comment'></div>开之于今，兼以其名，是以甚于古圣贤人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147908_comment'></div>明公得不念之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147908_comment'></div>茍明公不以二三小人之毁而移听于开，即开之名出于明公门下也，万万敢自贺曰必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147908_comment'></div>开再拜<span class='inlineComment2'>（《河东先生集》卷七。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147908_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1147908'>上句「毁我先君者」及此句「赵公」原阙，据彭本、傅本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1147908_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=973&endYear=973')">973年三月</a>　进士及第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5dfc4758563646ef8066a35d9bafd683_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5dfc4758563646ef8066a35d9bafd683");'><span id='5dfc4758563646ef8066a35d9bafd683_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年</a>，33岁</div><div id='5dfc4758563646ef8066a35d9bafd683' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年</a>　归，与潘阆、宋白、寇准等游。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3d8d4aa060d141da9bddba6578e216d2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3d8d4aa060d141da9bddba6578e216d2");'><span id='3d8d4aa060d141da9bddba6578e216d2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>，40岁</div><div id='3d8d4aa060d141da9bddba6578e216d2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年年初</a>　上蔡任上，率县民馈军粮到京师，上书求牵复。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='011d487bc4704a7da53902ae71a81296_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("011d487bc4704a7da53902ae71a81296");'><span id='011d487bc4704a7da53902ae71a81296_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>出知全州，自谓为赵昌言所累。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b7665275a7014807ac09592e893b8359_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年夏</a>　抵京师，有诗赠诸进士。作品：《赠诸进士诗》<div id='poem_179339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠诸进士诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（991年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_179339")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_179339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179339'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179339'>今年举进士，必谁登高第。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179339'>孙传及孙仅<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：孙传改名何。）</span>，外复有丁谓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179339'>到京见陈访，好尚同韩洎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179339'>馆中诸仙郎，纶閤贤三字。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179339'>翰林四主人，列辟群英粹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_179339'>厝腾走大名，淜轰天邑沸。<div id='poem_sentence_5_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_179339'>怒浪航斯济，骏蹄御良辔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_179339'>缘险径梯空，饿肠劳填味。<div id='poem_sentence_7_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_179339'>我何为欣欢，名身苦将悴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_179339'>北塞绝戎勋，南荒政遭坠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_179339'>焦焦家殚穷，口众食增累。<div id='poem_sentence_10_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_179339'>雏豝馀十辈，业学莫能器。<div id='poem_sentence_11_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_179339'>发白壮心衰，不觉老之至。<div id='poem_sentence_12_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_179339'>跼缩步九衢，羞畏同腐婢。<div id='poem_sentence_13_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_179339'>仰瞻尔数子，吾道终焉寄。<div id='poem_sentence_14_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_179339'>无为忽于予，斯文幸专继<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《河东先生集》卷一三）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_179339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_179339'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_179339_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年冬</a>　因全州黥徒事下狱四个月，勒停并追夺官职。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='53ff121e376b4b56933c5c200ee14f83_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("53ff121e376b4b56933c5c200ee14f83");'><span id='53ff121e376b4b56933c5c200ee14f83_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=993&endYear=993')">993年</a>，47岁</div><div id='53ff121e376b4b56933c5c200ee14f83' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>为传真大师元蔼作真赞。作品：《内供奉传真大师元蔼自写真赞》《真赞》<div id='poem_1147962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内供奉传真大师元蔼自写真赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（993年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147962")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147962'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147962'>蔼公来自蜀，以写真事求见上，上爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147962_comment'></div>自上而下，王公卿大夫士闻于时者，皆写之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147962_comment'></div>上命曰：「若能自写乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147962_comment'></div>曰：「能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147962_comment'></div>既成，观曰：「善」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147962_comment'></div>柳开见之，为作赞云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1147962'>他人写真，能写他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147962_comment'></div>蔼公自写，亦他人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147962_comment'></div>凝睇隐默，纤无差忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147962_comment'></div>至艺天与，超今迈古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147962_comment'></div>立名宋朝，万世之标。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1147962_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1147963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147963' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147963?labeling=true' target='_blank'>真赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（993年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147963")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147963'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147963'>淳化四年，开为蔼师自写真与作赞，蔼为开自作赞与写真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147963_comment'></div>赞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1147963'>仰匪高，修宁厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147963_comment'></div>识寡偶，志难就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147963_comment'></div>东西师，溪岩友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147963_comment'></div>审形义，非妍陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147963_comment'></div>圣如知，庆无咎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1147963_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b56c5f4ae30849ee86e31a81599b0586_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b56c5f4ae30849ee86e31a81599b0586");'><span id='b56c5f4ae30849ee86e31a81599b0586_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年</a>，48岁</div><div id='b56c5f4ae30849ee86e31a81599b0586' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=994&endYear=994')">994年冬</a>　诏归。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
镇江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3b710013337f4e578be4ec214d6b06f3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3b710013337f4e578be4ec214d6b06f3");'><span id='3b710013337f4e578be4ec214d6b06f3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=983')">980-983年</a>，34-37岁</div><div id='3b710013337f4e578be4ec214d6b06f3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年冬</a>　移知润州，拜监察御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年</a>　润州任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年六月</a>　丁母忧，有诏起复儒林郎，未离任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年春</a>　潘阆寄诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年八月</a>　重修润州孔庙成，为作碑文。作品：《润州重修文宣王庙碑文》<div id='poem_1147966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>润州重修文宣王庙碑文</a><span class='authorDate'>（983年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147966")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147966'>时称圣人之德者，多比以天地，为较量而言，盖以其至大故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147966_comment'></div>天地之有形，横亘太虚中计亿万里不啻，日月星辰、山川草木附而生之，赓亿万世，维固维存，是可为其大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147966_comment'></div>一旦或毁而不见，其大也何有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147966_comment'></div>先圣孔子，身长九尺六寸，寿年七十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147966_comment'></div>恓恓为旅人，为陪臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147966_comment'></div>作《诗》、《书》、大《易》、《春秋》、《礼记》之书，取三才洎万物，经而纬之，极其道者，不越于数言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147966_comment'></div>身非天地之广，寿非天地之永，殁而且久，终古益赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147966_comment'></div>以是而言，斯与天地并德而称大也，天地其无间然乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147966_comment'></div>天地尚如此，矧馀者可与孔子为其等伦也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147966_comment'></div>历代帝王，能知之者，乃立像貌，建宫庭，以时祠祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147966_comment'></div>尊之甚者，则封之以王爵命，被之以王衮冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147966_comment'></div>自国都至州县，庙学生徒，诏使如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147966_comment'></div>唐季失道，强夫戾顽，割裂土田，竞专制令，梁、周五代，弗克除削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147966_comment'></div>我太祖始愤起斩伐，得十八年，下荆，取湖，降蜀，擒广州，剋江南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147966_comment'></div>政修官严，物完兵强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147966_comment'></div>圣天子今绍服神休，召吴越瓯闽来走归我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147966_comment'></div>不四年，又尽平晋地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147966_comment'></div>万方六合，刬刷涤荡，悉绝纤垢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147966_comment'></div>润州在江南为上郡，有孔子庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147966_comment'></div>当僭伪时，阙法式，莫肯崇葺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147966_comment'></div>兼以提卒荷戈，拔剪疆垒，日蹂蹋作，落然芜秽，弗堪周视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147966_comment'></div>继莅长任辈，辜慠偷剥，宁曾少思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147966_comment'></div>太平兴国五年冬，开自常州知军州事授敕知此州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147966_comment'></div>吏盗贪羸，检夷澄育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147966_comment'></div>八年，政事简，秋八月哉生明，撤旧创新，告迁其庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147966_comment'></div>自颜子及孟子已下门人大儒之像，各塑缋配享于座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147966_comment'></div>厥功成，乃刻辞于石以纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147966_comment'></div>文曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1147966'>谓民无知，斯实乃欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147966_comment'></div>庙成来观，其乐怡怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147966_comment'></div>叹嗟兴言，严师崇教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147966_comment'></div>以齿以胄，我将子效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147966_comment'></div>里门郊路，出入谨让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147966_comment'></div>晨趋夕息，归所背向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147966_comment'></div>不争不踣，安用刑克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147966_comment'></div>移之四方，可则而康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147966_comment'></div>日升于天，视察明分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147966_comment'></div>霾蔀霄黑，其何为德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147966_comment'></div>伊谁谋之，曰开曰适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147966_comment'></div>适位宫官，判州通职<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147966_comment'></div>率吏奔工，九旬乃毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147966_comment'></div>仰瞻庶贤，群侍翼侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147966_comment'></div>拜祭堂下，伏泪如雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147966_comment'></div>惟圣成身，岂同父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147966_comment'></div>罔识得生，肖类毛羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147966_comment'></div>冠衣廪俸，帝锡而用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147966_comment'></div>言政行训，从学道重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147966_comment'></div>以报之恩，新此像宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147966_comment'></div>家兴礼仪，若鲁之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147966_comment'></div>当明天子，以文求士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147966_comment'></div>诰诏八纮，宁弗如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147966_comment'></div>复古尊儒，去夷即雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147966_comment'></div>化行来格，皆为达者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1147966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1147966'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_38_1147966_0'>⑴ 右赞善大夫、通判军州事张适同修此庙。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1147966_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年十二月</a>　赵晟前来代任，作书与赵。作品：《与起居舍人赵晟书》<div id='poem_1147911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147911?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与起居舍人赵晟书</a><span class='authorDate'>（983年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147911")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147911'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147911'>十二月日，从表弟起复儒林郎、守监察御史、知润州军州事柳开，再拜奉书于为光足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147911_comment'></div>为交友，有少为学时得之者，有壮而仕得之者，亦有迨老而后得之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147911_comment'></div>能以终若始之心不相负，是可谓君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147911_comment'></div>矧居时以势利万状，攻击而不能隐默，抵突则不足自保，斯何为言人也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147911_comment'></div>少而能得之，全其道，善可称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147911_comment'></div>虽若是，少时或相同，而后有达有不达者，有若贵若贱、若存若亡者，于其分亦所未备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147911_comment'></div>茍以少以壮以老皆相似，又有联隔阻异，望望不得且接近，终身言以病之，亦惟其可惜之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147911_comment'></div>开年十八，从烈考御史来京师，始与为光相遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147911_comment'></div>当此时，为光承顺于先尚书公左右，亦迨馀冠岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147911_comment'></div>一见甚相得，各自谓古人直不及我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147911_comment'></div>而后为光中进士第，历濠、襄两郡幕下，登朝迁拾遗、补阙，适广、桂诸部，得转运副使，连知虔、徐二州，任起居舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147911_comment'></div>开亦窃进士科名，选授宋州右司寇，稍迁录事参军，为太子右赞善大夫、殿中丞，两为监察御史，知常、润二州军州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147911_comment'></div>省而自念之，虽出处踪迹皆不及为光清峻显焕，然其不至寒饿，遑遑走四海尘土中，卑且贱，亦小可道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147911_comment'></div>开来润州三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147911_comment'></div>坐此地，日以官事细屑，政刑不敢少弛之，严帝典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147911_comment'></div>诸父诸母兄嫂氏没世不一，葬事间迄今不及，非人子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147911_comment'></div>每时思之，恨不能死，泣于天地，为无告矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147911_comment'></div>昨日得进奏院状，报为光授命实来替予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147911_comment'></div>喜感交乱于胸怀中，若戈戟亿卒斗蹋混走，莫可帖止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147911_comment'></div>为光为光，曾念之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147911_comment'></div>开与为光，故人也，岂不少而学时得相交友耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147911_comment'></div>趋进于名利之途，及第历官，曾是其贵贱、穷通、存亡殊然相远耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147911_comment'></div>迨此二十年，虽前后多不相见，今而来也，代予之任矣，询予之政矣，总予旧之民官吏兵矣，处予居之庭堂门路矣，役予信之仆圉阍守矣，用予作之罍皿檠洗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147911_comment'></div>子新晨入矣，予前夕行矣，憯然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147911_comment'></div>虽以是不能久相待焉，方之望望不得接近，又可庶之免也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147911_comment'></div>况信守之，义成之，礼节之，仁和之，炳然不相欺愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147911_comment'></div>今日之前，似合其道也，得相视一欢笑，无怨怼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147911_comment'></div>今日之后，况与为光各省识时事，肯为不及于前日乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147911_comment'></div>可无忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147911_comment'></div>若是其他人视之，得无谓予与为光能全其交之美者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147911_comment'></div>方舟远来，涉彼淮江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147911_comment'></div>寒风凄其，劳动兴止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147911_comment'></div>衙吏命往，公仆载迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147911_comment'></div>军州故事，容悉陈启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147911_comment'></div>相见不远，欣然莫休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147911_comment'></div>仲涂顿首再拜。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1147911'></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1147911_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
清河
