-----title
上蔡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e005ad2266ad44b4bcbb28eb05443591_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e005ad2266ad44b4bcbb28eb05443591");'><span id='e005ad2266ad44b4bcbb28eb05443591_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>，39岁</div><div id='e005ad2266ad44b4bcbb28eb05443591' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　在上蔡任，以兴利爱民为务。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bb46d60e2d794fd9a11889b17362848c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb46d60e2d794fd9a11889b17362848c");'><span id='bb46d60e2d794fd9a11889b17362848c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>，40岁</div><div id='bb46d60e2d794fd9a11889b17362848c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年二月十一日</a>　上书吕蒙正，乞行非常之恩。作品：《上参政吕给事书》<div id='poem_1147913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上参政吕给事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年二月十一日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147913")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147913_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147913'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147913'>二月十一日，将仕郎、守蔡州上蔡县令柳开，谨献书于执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147913_comment'></div>人之罪莫大于不忠不孝，开今有之，得以言于执事，执事必听而信矣，哀而怜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147913_comment'></div>夫国家以科第爵位取士者，要欲安民治国，扶树教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147913_comment'></div>自千百人中，始得一人登名礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147913_comment'></div>自礼部由吏部为州县吏，复于千百人中，始得一人登名朝籍，立之于明廷，居之以显位，出入受寄，承天子宰相指画，理平小大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147913_comment'></div>是乃求人任官，非为易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147913_comment'></div>其有轻而弃之，自取败祸者，岂得为忠乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147913_comment'></div>开一举中进士第，凡五年为吏郡府，而入朝四迁五命，得殿中侍御史，三典大州，受皇朝名位非不重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147913_comment'></div>而一旦不忍小忿，与人任气争斗，紊烦上心，削去朝籍，逐为县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147913_comment'></div>不能重主上之命而固守名器，辱君父任使之意，名书刑籍，使万方议而笑之，以为国家任非其人，斯开不忠之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147913_comment'></div>开父任监察御史，乾德三年卒于泗州官舍，至雍熙甲申岁，二十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147913_comment'></div>其间开母氏洎叔父三人、叔母氏、兄辟与诸嫂氏，又七人相继亡殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147913_comment'></div>开以游学从宦，生计牢落，竟未能克襄葬事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147913_comment'></div>又幼弟稚妹，婚嫁失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147913_comment'></div>开在江南数年，每一念至，不觉心神绝死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147913_comment'></div>前年，开自知润州得替归京，以家在河北，曾具此二事白于政事堂，中蒙执事赐以贝州之命，开甚为获所愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147913_comment'></div>到治所后，方经营婚葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147913_comment'></div>不三月，长兄闵卒于昭义军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147913_comment'></div>又不两月间，次兄肩吾自知郢州罢还阙下，行次唐州而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147913_comment'></div>后不十旬，开以兵马都监赵嘉进监押翟廷玉，以官事苦相侵逼，致各忿争，天怒降威，追官作宰，窘辱颠沛，极不忍言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147913_comment'></div>向所求来河北营度迁葬婚嫁事，无所能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147913_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147913_comment'></div>开为人子，父母叔婶兄嫂氏计十四人死而不葬馀二十年，弟妹成人又失婚嫁，名辱身困，岂为孝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147913_comment'></div>斯开不孝之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147913_comment'></div>每念此事，开诚不忠不孝人也，罪亦大矣，生何为矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147913_comment'></div>直以诸孤孩孺累累满前，寒饿徬徨，家仅百口，非知开而大有力者，莫能救之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147913_comment'></div>开于执事，不敢言布衣旧常知开矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147913_comment'></div>今天下大臣中立朝廷受上知者，唯执事一人为最，位居相府，名动寰区，亦大有力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147913_comment'></div>若是，而非执事者不能救开矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147913_comment'></div>执事非此时也，即又不能大施其力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147913_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147913_comment'></div>凡上之施恩威于下有非常者，必上不能直行而专为也，必左右有以非常之善恶先闻于上也，然后上乃行非常之威以罚恶，非常之恩以赏善耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147913_comment'></div>开昨获罪，实甚非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147913_comment'></div>开今仰望于执事者，望执事以非常之善言闻于上，乞行非常之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147913_comment'></div>况以执事当此非常之时，有非常之便，可以行非常之惠，救非常之辜于开也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147913_comment'></div>开闻方今大发师徒，必有征伐，是非常之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147913_comment'></div>国家事繁务众，文武要人，是非常之便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147913_comment'></div>执事若念开昨触犯刑章，无毫发赃贿，上不负国，下不侵民，止以王事与同职争竞，审言于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147913_comment'></div>又开平燕袭晋之年，催运楚、泗八州，及起遣镇州粮草八十万计，随驾先行，皆获周旋无误，前后任使，咸以干局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147913_comment'></div>言之具列于上，乞于今时重难极处，使之以赎前罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147913_comment'></div>如此，是执事可以行非常之惠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147913_comment'></div>倘执事力言于上，取开于下，舍其罪戾，役以重难，离此州县之中，再列班行之末，是救开非常之辜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147913_comment'></div>若执事因此时垂大惠，即救开甚为易耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147913_comment'></div>若此时执事不赐哀怜，特加振拔，即开无缘免此危困穷戚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147913_comment'></div>惴惴旦暮，死亡可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147913_comment'></div>若过此时，俟于他日，执事纵欲致开于无过之地，救开于久困之涂，亦难为力，而无其便矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147913_comment'></div>直写危恳，且陈短书，号伏尘泥，朝夕望命，唯执事悯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147913_comment'></div>开死罪死罪。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1147913'></div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1147913_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年三月六日</a>　上书李昉，自称“受恩门下”作品：《上史馆相公书》<div id='poem_1147914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147914?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上史馆相公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年三月六日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147914")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147914'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147914'>三月六日，将仕郎、守蔡州上蔡县令柳开，谨沥血献书于相公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147914_comment'></div>人于天不可得而升，得升于天者，凡骨为仙，知不死于尘世耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147914_comment'></div>开于京城不可得而见，开今得至于京城，得见于相公，即灾害可免，穷困可伸，脱出泥滓之中，再登霄汉之上，知不难矣，与其升天为仙，其亦不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147914_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147914_comment'></div>开负罪南迁，逐为县令，囚系下位，愁忧日煎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147914_comment'></div>骨肉之间，疾病太半，俸薄家贫，食不充饱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147914_comment'></div>父母没世，闭骨浅草，弟妹婚嫁，绝无遂心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147914_comment'></div>茫茫天地之中，开为厄穷极矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147914_comment'></div>开去年以不忍小忿，与同职以王事争斗，上辱皇帝任使之意，下玷相公变化之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147914_comment'></div>虽不犯赃，虽不负国，虽不怠慢公事，虽不侵害黎民，其如君子用和，儒者立行，即何远乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147914_comment'></div>斯开自致之罪戾亦极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147914_comment'></div>厄穷且如是，罪戾亦如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147914_comment'></div>若守职在县，夐隔路途，虽欲言之于相公，无由得至京城矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147914_comment'></div>今来率领部民，馈辇军食，路出天阙，迹达相门，即诚可陈，事可谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147914_comment'></div>开受恩门下已十五年，相公忍不哀而念之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147914_comment'></div>况相公积仁累行，亘围物表，草木虫鱼，尚加惠养，况于开反肯无情乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147914_comment'></div>斯开自知免灾害，化穷困，出泥滓，上霄汉，在相公一言有馀，知不难于今日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147914_comment'></div>是行也，开变祸为福，易愁为娱，期之朝夕，自可前贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147914_comment'></div>凡遭逢天命之归己者，帝王之位可得；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147914_comment'></div>遭逢人主之用己者，将相之位可得；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147914_comment'></div>遭逢宰相之知己者，公卿之位可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147914_comment'></div>古人与今人穷达，此理一致耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147914_comment'></div>无如是有遭逢者，求而且为难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147914_comment'></div>上天景命，下属圣君，万方承平，远绝古昔，是天命永归于皇家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147914_comment'></div>高坐庙堂，密运筹策，子视稷、契，奴命萧、曹，是人主之大用相公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147914_comment'></div>开自应举历官，出入门下，屈伸动静，钜细承恩，是遭逢于相公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147914_comment'></div>而开不能慎守名器，大掇悔尤，退黜朝行，沉落坑阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147914_comment'></div>茍无此事，即相公于开也，岂惜公卿之位乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147914_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147914_comment'></div>每一念之，不觉心死，古谓噬脐不及者，正在开耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147914_comment'></div>惟相公悯察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147914_comment'></div>茍不垂惠，则柳氏之族必也衰亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147914_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1147914_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='11c7d8910330486c98c0e11da3432c43_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("11c7d8910330486c98c0e11da3432c43");'><span id='11c7d8910330486c98c0e11da3432c43_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>，40岁</div><div id='11c7d8910330486c98c0e11da3432c43' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年夏五月</a>　随兵回，告高頔孤，愿为高頔作墓铭。作品：《高頔墓志铭》<div id='poem_1147978' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147978' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147978?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故中大夫左补阙致仕高公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年夏五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147978")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147978_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147978'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147978'>郡府间年贡士上列，宰相择辞臣、学官，躬五试之岁，岁三月甲子，渤海高南金，治毛、郑《诗》，中第，在殿方引卷召名，上视之曰：「高书记子乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147978_comment'></div>大臣覆之，曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147978_comment'></div>上曰：「頔在乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147978_comment'></div>当老矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147978_comment'></div>南金对曰：「臣父年八十一，在矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147978_comment'></div>上曰：「朕昔迎后<span class='inlineComment2'>（符氏）</span>，抵魏，王命頔曰佐朕膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147978_comment'></div>頔上手不懈，兢兢然，多礼人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147978_comment'></div>大臣交赞荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147978_comment'></div>退呼南金问者三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147978_comment'></div>上曰：「授汝父左补阙其致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147978_comment'></div>吾旌善人，用劝天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147978_comment'></div>致仕官无俸入，赐钱十万，令于魏取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147978_comment'></div>翌日，南金捧命来归，公拜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147978_comment'></div>幕府吏动天子加殊命，非常者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147978_comment'></div>夏五月，开自贝贬逐南行，过公宇下，见公冠大顶乌纱叠帽，衣缁缘褐縠单裘，手右曳杖，左捧囊，中出锦引幅，茜牙轴，纹绫背纸押，押第署朱镂印文，披之，即新诰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147978_comment'></div>公持之如不胜，感涕下𧸘，荷君至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147978_comment'></div>明年春三月丁丑，开率县民馈军伐燕，路出大名，乡之人语开曰：「公当去月辛酉殁矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147978_comment'></div>夏五月庚寅，开随兵回，使告其孤曰：「愿铭公墓，以报公厚知于我也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147978_comment'></div>润、南金与鼎三子，列公行事以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147978_comment'></div>唐建中年，太常为七岁女子以父彦昭事能死贼中，谥之为悯，名曰妹妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147978_comment'></div>彦昭守濮阳，背贼纳归于德宗，封平恩郡王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147978_comment'></div>生同州文学讳衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147978_comment'></div>衡生西吾，隐而不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147978_comment'></div>西吾生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147978_comment'></div>公字子奇，用文取进士高第，历慈丘、遂平二主簿，安、申等州，大名府观察两支使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147978_comment'></div>周显德中，魏王奏授公掌书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147978_comment'></div>开宝二年，王移凤翔府，至洛，帝止之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147978_comment'></div>公从王罢归，复选授旧官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147978_comment'></div>六年，丁太夫人琅邪王氏忧，终丧足不越庭户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147978_comment'></div>府帅李公复奏公如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147978_comment'></div>上二年，有诬奏公以老而怠其任者，急诏庭见责之，辞不小屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147978_comment'></div>上曰：「尔实止为一书记，其久而曾无莅他事乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147978_comment'></div>公对曰：「臣守道俟命，不茍不竞，乃如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147978_comment'></div>府钜细事无官者，臣兼治之，非止在臣所职书记耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147978_comment'></div>上曰：「若何谓頔老不治务乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147978_comment'></div>尔去，复其位矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147978_comment'></div>七年，公始以疾免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147978_comment'></div>昔王之未去府也，左右惟贪虐取下，下所不能堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147978_comment'></div>及王之去，即羞惧无敢一游于魏者，独公居之，前后三十年，不迁不离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147978_comment'></div>始至之日，与告终之夕，出处进退，语默用舍，无革无愧，人无咎言，世谓公君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147978_comment'></div>公至魏之初，有群小吏遇公于涂中，趋而候公，公即停驾揖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147978_comment'></div>有大吏复若是，公乃降，答以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147978_comment'></div>至公免职，公固不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147978_comment'></div>以是吏多避去，不敢见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147978_comment'></div>与公言，经史子集，举而问之，则公恳恳诵之，无有舛忘，皆如目前事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147978_comment'></div>公为文精且典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147978_comment'></div>手抄书千卷，字细如豆，无漏无误，老而益精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147978_comment'></div>得之者，藏为书宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147978_comment'></div>信义忠勇，孝爱仁恕，公不阙一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147978_comment'></div>公长子浣暨公夫人赵郡李氏，先公而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147978_comment'></div>某年月日，以公归大名府元城县某乡某里李夫人之坟葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147978_comment'></div>公三女：孟适故兴元府司录参军晁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147978_comment'></div>仲适将作监丞李策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147978_comment'></div>季适著作佐郎集用砺，未归而夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147978_comment'></div>南金解褐，得沙河尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147978_comment'></div>鼎应进士举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147978_comment'></div>公卒之日无恙，教诫后事不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147978_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1147978'>群万浩浩，公独有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147978_comment'></div>驱谀竞偷，公学优优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1147978_comment'></div>易世一官，行积名完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1147978_comment'></div>公之所易，人之所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1147978_comment'></div>赀充位崇，死矣其空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1147978_comment'></div>方之在公，我殊彼同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1147978_comment'></div>以诰何慝，乃褒何德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1147978_comment'></div>岁纪未极，斯焉消息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1147978_comment'></div>惟天聪明，视谛听诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1147978_comment'></div>凑声渊穆，无适莫程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1147978_comment'></div>埃坌窒目，奔夷且覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1147978_comment'></div>纳吉必经，反危以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1147978_comment'></div>此之云远，其逝不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1147978_comment'></div>岂惟于人，亦惟于身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1147978_comment'></div>我来旧乡，公今云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1147978_comment'></div>厥善其长，厥裔其昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1147978_comment'></div>写我心伤，刻为辞章。</div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1147978_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　致书李宗谔，并评其文。作品：《与李宗谔秀才书》<div id='poem_1147920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李宗谔秀才书</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147920")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147920'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147920'>秀才足下：贤愚之生，无择其所处也，惟其人在乎心别耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147920_comment'></div>文章之所主，道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147920_comment'></div>古之为学，公卿士大夫之子弟，立身行道，取位与名，必用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147920_comment'></div>后之公卿士大夫之子弟，惟取位为丰逸之具，乃罕学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147920_comment'></div>其学者，非章句浅末之类，求第有司，进明天子者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147920_comment'></div>学谓立言垂教，行义炳炳，如古贤君子耳，贵家子少专焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147920_comment'></div>专之者，惟穷悴孑孑，介特寒士，愤悱之不胜所作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147920_comment'></div>贵家子能此者，自汉而下四十年，开能识者，为足下一言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147920_comment'></div>周末故范鲁公为相国，子弟中惟今杲立节好学，相国洎朝之百执事，以至后进群生，皆知而奇待焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147920_comment'></div>乃至今来，以文得名，以文得位，居贫御众，能偕古人有道，惟杲可尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147920_comment'></div>四十年中得相位者，仅十家，而其淳诚遗直，材略杰异，不贪不佞，巍然有良相之风者，亦惟鲁公耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147920_comment'></div>十家子有亡有存，于今为世言者有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147920_comment'></div>得位齿于卿大夫者，于今复有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147920_comment'></div>其为名不时异者，与不得位而泯没者，斯无异也，孰偕杲哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147920_comment'></div>此无他，惟学与不学耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147920_comment'></div>去年春在贝州，有幕吏刘去华，新拜观察推官之命而来郡中，开始见之，辞气恢然，举止详熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147920_comment'></div>间求其所从来，即其道出于贤尊相公之门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147920_comment'></div>召与之语，即数数称足下行事不类于贵家子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147920_comment'></div>言足下出即乘蹇驴，张弊盖，从小仆，不佩文犀诸金具，带、衣惟纯色常服；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147920_comment'></div>言不哗妄，心能别是非，有信义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147920_comment'></div>耽学好文，文之辞章卓异峻拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147920_comment'></div>居其家，相国多器之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147920_comment'></div>与士大夫群进后生游，众必推尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147920_comment'></div>开当闻之时，诚欲识足下面耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147920_comment'></div>今年春，过京师，托进士崔景言之于足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147920_comment'></div>开所志者，愿与足下为一时之交，非求媚也，直欲与足下使世称谓叹美，以道相得耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147920_comment'></div>中执宪赵公在魏时，开于今夏中日得奉于左右，常言足下为今时之俊人伟才，将特荐进于上，要足下赞教化，惠邦家，为天下之雄冠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147920_comment'></div>开今来得复旧官，留于京邑，思与足下朝夕游处，各尽其所怀，以其事役劬劬，卒未得相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147920_comment'></div>数日前，崔秀才袖足下文一轴及《永泰门义井铭》石本一篇见贶，读之竟日，知称咏足下者不为谬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147920_comment'></div>足下之文雅而理明白，气和且清，真可贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147920_comment'></div>足下若不废于学，勤勤然，即至于道，其不难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147920_comment'></div>名称禄位，必由己立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147920_comment'></div>十数年外，可与杲为敌耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147920_comment'></div>贵家子群不能远望辙迹，况能踵哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147920_comment'></div>贤尊相公懿德洪业，近年无及，真又与鲁公不相上下，是知四十年间，惟足下与范两家父子为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147920_comment'></div>后之视今，犹今视昔也，足下惟勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147920_comment'></div>开俟足下成之惟速，冀后人仰望足下清尘，知开言为不佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147920_comment'></div>开性直好古，立朝且孤，与之朋游，罕见其类，志之大者，望于足下耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147920_comment'></div>所遗文谨留为好，请无赐罪让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147920_comment'></div>开白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1147920_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　出使河北，曾飞章奏边事，又上《陈情表》作品：《上太宗皇帝陈情表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　上书王承衍，主张以诈、奇、谋、勇抵御辽兵。作品：《上王太保书》<div id='poem_1147904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147904?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上王太保书</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147904")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147904'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147904'>兵者以诈行，以奇胜，以谋先，以勇固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147904_comment'></div>失此四者，败之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147904_comment'></div>开生长河朔间，读书为文之外，好寻前古兴亡成败之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147904_comment'></div>自儿童时，复见烈考每每话后唐庄宗迄于晋、汉朝与北虏战争之事，历历如在眼前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147904_comment'></div>开今夏中随兵馈粮，北抵涿州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147904_comment'></div>观其北虏用兵之法，皆如往昔烈考所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147904_comment'></div>察其国家将卒之徒，即有异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147904_comment'></div>以朝廷自周世宗取淮南，收秦凤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147904_comment'></div>太祖皇帝下荆湖，破西川、广南，灭吴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147904_comment'></div>皇帝平晋与吴越、瓯闽，三十年中，兵出即胜，谋动即成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147904_comment'></div>今天朝兵虽多，将虽众，其为争胜之道，视北虏犹视吴、蜀、晋、楚之师，所以开谓其有异而乃失其利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147904_comment'></div>北虏非吴、蜀、晋、楚之匹也：用非诈也，不能及其心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147904_comment'></div>出非奇也，不能敌其众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147904_comment'></div>动非谋也，不能防其奸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147904_comment'></div>战非勇也，不能捍其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147904_comment'></div>轻而视之，易而行之，非所以利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147904_comment'></div>北虏昨自祁沟之役洎此，入数月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147904_comment'></div>逐我师而回，乘胜也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147904_comment'></div>念己地之侵，蓄怒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147904_comment'></div>乘胜而蓄怒，今其来也，必选其劲虏精骑，尽率其群，决入吾境，势甚锐耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147904_comment'></div>刘与李不能坚壁清野，备而避之，非善之将者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147904_comment'></div>譬之恶兽，有暴其巢窟者，退必咆哮攫齧，肆害于物，当此之时，未可制其横猾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147904_comment'></div>茍俟其怒心发极之后，从而图之，可为易耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147904_comment'></div>今闻北虏尚在瀛州界内，开计其来也，肯此而退乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147904_comment'></div>虏使间者南入深、冀，先行侦察也，勿以其寂然无声，谓其息也，此乃谋其往耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147904_comment'></div>勿以其居然不动，谓其止也，此乃窥其便耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147904_comment'></div>今明公承命而来，禁旅旋至，开欲乞候兵师到此，即请尽出甲兵，多持旌旗，缓行而前，至府北属县已来，扬声云大军数十万相次而至，夜即多以火鼓，张其兵势，仍请分命两道而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147904_comment'></div>北面城邑军兵，闻必增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147904_comment'></div>若贼虏有南顾之心，闻之必未敢轻易而进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147904_comment'></div>若贼虏本无南顾之心，此行不远而回，又且无害于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147904_comment'></div>况大河之北，郡县累累，民居相邻，户仅百万，闻王师而大至，其心宁不顿得安乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147904_comment'></div>俟其旬浃间，城池修完，北虏不进，即请明公相度乞圣驾行幸天雄军驻跸，而后进军，渐抵贝、冀，声援边方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147904_comment'></div>若得北虏退归，河朔无事，即却贼安边之功，尽成明公之勋业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147904_comment'></div>开儒学议兵，不识远大，僭易闻启，惶惧实深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147904_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1147904_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
博野
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3aaebc3253374c7082d954b66b6e6d80_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3aaebc3253374c7082d954b66b6e6d80");'><span id='3aaebc3253374c7082d954b66b6e6d80_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=988')">987-988年</a>，41-42岁</div><div id='3aaebc3253374c7082d954b66b6e6d80' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年七月</a>　知宁边军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　赴边时，潘阆有诗相赠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年十二月</a>　上书郭守文，料契丹不至犯边。作品：《上郭太傅书》<div id='poem_1147917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上郭太傅书</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147917")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147917'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147917'>十二月十五日，崇仪使、知宁边军柳开，谨再拜，献书于宣徽太傅旌旗之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147917_comment'></div>今月八日，殿直张维恩走马赍到雄、霸等诸州军探到蕃贼排比，恐犯边境事宜，不同众状，转牒一道，令开子细探候者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147917_comment'></div>开本儒官，于兵家事苦不深会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147917_comment'></div>幸逢圣主擢为近臣，承倚毗于边，方令捍御其丑虏，在七擒七纵而未展，于知彼知己以粗能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147917_comment'></div>开昨独不曾有状申报蕃贼恐入界者，开缘料得蕃贼此者不来犯边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147917_comment'></div>其事有五：一，天顺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147917_comment'></div>二，时晚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147917_comment'></div>三，地困；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147917_comment'></div>四，人牢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147917_comment'></div>五，势怯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147917_comment'></div>天顺者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147917_comment'></div>兵主杀，杀主阴，阴主凄惨、寒烈、晦冥、昏霾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147917_comment'></div>今冬已来，天日晴暖，郁郁如春，无严风，无苦雪，无惨雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147917_comment'></div>昼夜视之，彼贼上无云无气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147917_comment'></div>每每南首而望，我云如堤如林，横亘天际，极高极厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147917_comment'></div>河冰不坚，随日融释；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147917_comment'></div>太阴夜晕，胡星昼掩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147917_comment'></div>凡兵动有战，破军杀将，即天须示变于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147917_comment'></div>今上天如此，是为天顺，而开所以知其不来者，此为一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147917_comment'></div>时晚者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147917_comment'></div>高秋草肥，馀粮在野，马壮弓劲，分路齐驱，若彼时蕃贼南行，堪为我患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147917_comment'></div>今则岁已暮冬，至春不远，大兵若动，进退经时，彼若暂来便回，彼即有害无利，虚成劳众，无以近人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147917_comment'></div>此是为时晚，而开所以知其不来者二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147917_comment'></div>地困者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147917_comment'></div>蕃贼用兵，务食于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147917_comment'></div>天资皇帝圣智，河北千里内村野间，民家刍粟粮储，宣命并已收拾入城，坡野众草烧爇欲尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147917_comment'></div>彼贼若来，既无辇运，何能赡兵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147917_comment'></div>且以三五万骑胡兵计之，日用粮草颇众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147917_comment'></div>攻城池，又城池已固；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147917_comment'></div>掠村野，又村野皆空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147917_comment'></div>久住又计日无可支持，轻行又逐处恐遭掩杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147917_comment'></div>况其大众，何以能行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147917_comment'></div>此是地困，而开所以知其不来者三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147917_comment'></div>人牢者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147917_comment'></div>逐处城池，屯兵甚众，南至澶、滑，师旅转多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147917_comment'></div>去年河北军民所被杀虏甚苦，此来怨惧，在处皆同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147917_comment'></div>怨者，怨杀虏于人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147917_comment'></div>惧者，惧杀虏到己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147917_comment'></div>皆能预备，例各齐心，缓则逐处宴安，急则逐处拒敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147917_comment'></div>此是为人牢，而开所以知其不来者四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147917_comment'></div>势怯者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147917_comment'></div>去冬瀛州我师败绩，彼贼首领乘胜破深州、下武强等县，将兵遽回，独耶律逊宁袭其空虚，破德州、滳河县而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147917_comment'></div>以其去冬城池不修，兵甲皆阙，村野无备，刍谷至多，贼兵尚且倏来而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147917_comment'></div>今岁河北城垒坚完，四望相属，戈甲如云，野无馀食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147917_comment'></div>茍来犯边，出入须惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147917_comment'></div>以其去冬尚怯，而今冬岂能勇乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147917_comment'></div>此是为其势怯，而开所以知其不来者五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147917_comment'></div>况皇帝圣神，为天下主，胡雏虏婢岂能敌乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147917_comment'></div>其雄、霸等州军所探得蕃贼排比，恐犯边者，必是蕃贼首领北归，扬其虚声，张其贼势，惧王师之袭后，所谓往而示之以来之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147917_comment'></div>兵行贵诈，古今自同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147917_comment'></div>且以匹夫之事喻之，而可知其不来之理明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1147917_comment'></div>今有下俚愚夫相聚，至甚尘微，而尚不肯轻出一辞，轻举一事，以为他先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1147917_comment'></div>而况大国大兵，而肯容易不顾利害而动哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1147917_comment'></div>不尔者，当是耶律逊宁为其本主不来犯边，要扇其事，诱动我师，反惑其主，欲固己之权与位耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1147917_comment'></div>小人怀奸，其心难知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1147917_comment'></div>皇王之道，混成如天，包笼四周，俾莫能越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1147917_comment'></div>明公赞辅圣帝，掌握精兵，料敌安边，如古名将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1147917_comment'></div>开愚直无识，祗以惊惭，辄具启闻，望赐悉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1147917_comment'></div>开顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1147917_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　知边宁军。作品：《塞上》<div id='poem_179333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>塞上</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_179333")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_179333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179333'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179333'>鸣髇直上一千尺，天静无风声更乾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179333'>碧眼胡儿三百骑，尽提金勒向云看<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179333'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_179333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_179333'><span class='label'>《宋朝事实类苑》：</span>冯太傅端尝书一绝句云云，顾坐客曰：此可画于屏障。乃柳如京《塞上》之作。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_179333_0'>⑴ 宋江少虞《宋朝事实类苑》卷三五引《倦游杂录》</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_179333_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年五月</a>　诏替归京，上书樊知古求留任河洛以营葬。作品：《与河北都转运樊谏议书》<div id='poem_1147915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与河北都转运樊谏议书</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147915")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147915'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147915'>五月七日，崇仪使柳开再拜，献书于谏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147915_comment'></div>人之事，系于情，极者无越于父与母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147915_comment'></div>不以尊卑疏密，可与不可，有往告而必告者，虽得死责，无悔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147915_comment'></div>大君子闻之，亦不以其尊卑疏密，可与不可，但能施其力者，亦当不惜耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147915_comment'></div>况其十年受顾瞩，非不为故旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147915_comment'></div>每侍坐左右，燕言无间，非不为深密也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147915_comment'></div>开言及此者，以开先父太祖朝乾德三年任监察御史，为泗州兵马钤辖、通判州事，夏五月得疾，卒于官舍，到此岁二十有四年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147915_comment'></div>其间仲父、叔父、季父、伯兄、仲兄、次兄，洎母氏、叔母氏、兄嫂氏，计一十五人相次亡殁，迄今未襄葬事，聚骨郊野垒垒，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147915_comment'></div>开于太平兴国九年，任监察御史，知润州军州归，求得知贝州，以其岁月日时将吉，且卜葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147915_comment'></div>至雍熙二年，开为殿中侍御史，春正月，因同职者以王事忿争，开追削朝籍，得上蔡县令，其葬事乃罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147915_comment'></div>至三年，开逐曹师馈粮伐燕，自涿州回，过阙下，献书乞从边军效死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147915_comment'></div>上念开前罪无大，故情可怜惜，复得殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147915_comment'></div>是岁也，奉使河北，冬十二月，值王师有瀛州之役，连城陷贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147915_comment'></div>开以河北事机飞章疾奏，上恕而纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147915_comment'></div>明年夏归，上于文吏中方求将兵者，开与墀、载辈首得预选，充崇仪使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147915_comment'></div>秋七月，方在邢州训练兵卒，急诏令知宁边军，所谓奋空拳而冒白刃，坐虎口而断贼臂也，众所知耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147915_comment'></div>柳，宫姓，今年岁得戊子，且利为葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147915_comment'></div>开又复得在河北，有上所赐中金可为充办，方经营于秋冬以襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147915_comment'></div>今者开诏替归京，复不知千里万里东南西北而往矣，其葬事今敢决而为望哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147915_comment'></div>是行也，父母叔婶兄嫂氏幽魂白骨其为厄乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147915_comment'></div>越此年后，得岁在丙申，柳姓始利为葬，计之有八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147915_comment'></div>八年间，身名禄位，开果自保必存乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147915_comment'></div>苟先风露，即岂不动大君子哀念之心哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147915_comment'></div>是开得在河北，即父母亲族间葬事不能营耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147915_comment'></div>惟明公忠于事君，孝于奉亲，义于友朋，惠于人民，所以开敢言而求其力耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147915_comment'></div>于上所言事必从者，非府主太尉石公不可矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147915_comment'></div>于府主石公言事必纳者，非明公不可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147915_comment'></div>开复见魏、博、慈、相等州都巡检使，岁月过满，开欲求而为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147915_comment'></div>乞明公于府主太尉一言之，望府主太尉一奏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147915_comment'></div>如此，则开必得在河朔间，于父母亲族亡没者一十五人，可为歛而今岁成葬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147915_comment'></div>是明公一言，而免此八年之晚，与先风露之忧，明公岂不动念哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147915_comment'></div>死者无知则其已矣，如有知也，岂不阴助明公而致福哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147915_comment'></div>况开之门有男夫长幼十九人矣，岂知他日无以国士报公者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147915_comment'></div>诚迫辞直，公其听悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147915_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1147915_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

扬州

<div class='label1' id='4342099cb6d84e88bc2699d515d9cf29_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4342099cb6d84e88bc2699d515d9cf29");'><span id='4342099cb6d84e88bc2699d515d9cf29_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>，42岁</div><div id='4342099cb6d84e88bc2699d515d9cf29' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　途出维扬，潘阆戏装鬼怪以怖之。<br /></div>

-----title
全州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6267fee6c47444d1975a25f9660125fd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6267fee6c47444d1975a25f9660125fd");'><span id='6267fee6c47444d1975a25f9660125fd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=989')">988-989年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='6267fee6c47444d1975a25f9660125fd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年六月十一日前</a>　已至全州任，郑景宗寄文，作书答之。作品：与郑景宗书》<div id='poem_1147916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147916?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与郑景宗书</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年六月十一日前）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147916")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147916'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147916'>唐高祖、太宗始命有司岁考郡县贡举人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147916_comment'></div>至昭宗，二百八十年间，所得名将、名相、贤人、哲士、卿大夫，皆自中而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147916_comment'></div>故延十八世，天下同正朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147916_comment'></div>纵天宝年后叛乱时起，而终不失承平基业者，以高祖、太宗能以文取士，尽海内之心如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147916_comment'></div>唐之政以文而弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147916_comment'></div>继唐者循袭不革，所以梁与后唐、晋、汉、周五代，皆不永长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147916_comment'></div>是不识事久即变，不变即虽帝皇为道，终难妥泰无事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147916_comment'></div>春夏秋冬，天地之为变，成岁时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147916_comment'></div>盈亏中昃，日月之为变，成昼夜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147916_comment'></div>是其为道者，有其变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147916_comment'></div>无变者，道之失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147916_comment'></div>太祖皇帝开宝六年，命今仆射李公考试贡举人，取士有不能尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147916_comment'></div>是时，太祖方尅意务理，思与前代英主并立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147916_comment'></div>然而刑政德业，世用不变于唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147916_comment'></div>春，进士徐士廉谋曰：「天子起艰难中，识艰难事，每外闻䊸横直捷，为梗为利，即薙刬增树，急如身病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147916_comment'></div>我当上言有司之不良，堙压中善，取快于帝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147916_comment'></div>且伏阙下，求见太祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147916_comment'></div>太祖召与之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147916_comment'></div>廉即具道贡举人事，请太祖廷试之，曰：「方今中外兵百万，提强黜弱，日决自上前，出无敢悖者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147916_comment'></div>惟岁取儒为吏官下百数，常常赘戾，以其授于人而不自决致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147916_comment'></div>为国家天下，止文与武二柄取士耳，无为其下鬻恩也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147916_comment'></div>太祖即命礼部试所中、不中贡举人列于殿廷试之，得百有二十七人，赐登高第，开幸在其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147916_comment'></div>后二年，廷试如六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147916_comment'></div>明年太祖崩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147916_comment'></div>今上即位，廷试事亦如太祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147916_comment'></div>然其优锡殊任，与太祖绝大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147916_comment'></div>盖上多文好学，知变而谋久者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147916_comment'></div>到于今，上凡八试天下士，获仅五千人，上自中书门下为宰相，下至县邑为簿尉，其间台省郡府、公卿大夫，悉见奇能异行，各竞为文武中俊臣，皆上之所取贡举人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147916_comment'></div>是与唐取士为用，此变而大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147916_comment'></div>唐高祖、太宗用文取士，止于委在有司，任之以大小吏职，亦止渐阶第进，殊无擢英拔秀，焕视惊听，朝为群儒，暮为群公者，尚能作固宗邦垂三百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147916_comment'></div>非如夫太祖纳人一言，变古易式，取由朕，弃由朕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147916_comment'></div>今上恢阐其道，广穷俊能，海外区中，良才硕士，皆自我得，材智取异，名位取大，傍睨下视，尹、夔、旦、奭，逐逐如儿子辈，即何止于百千万祀定其享天下乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147916_comment'></div>贤贤世世，齐天地为久耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147916_comment'></div>古之得一士者昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147916_comment'></div>「三人行，必有我师」，谓三人为众，众乃可有贤于圣者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147916_comment'></div>今上已八试贡举人，得五千人，何古之得一士可比也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147916_comment'></div>三人行，中有圣人之师者，可同也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1147916_comment'></div>斯五千人，其为众也，将不啻倍千于三人之行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1147916_comment'></div>是知得人之盛，无如于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1147916_comment'></div>开雍熙四年，过大名府，始遇足下新于上前以文得名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1147916_comment'></div>而客来河北，暂得相识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1147916_comment'></div>今来南岭之畔，蒙惠新文，捧读三四，见足下胸怀蕴奥，惠戴民君，志义超远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1147916_comment'></div>足见今上之得士，信不为不尽材也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1147916_comment'></div>万事古不能尽，随日生而多且新也，惟后来者，斯亦不之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1147916_comment'></div>唐高祖、太宗昔为求贤得尽士也，宁知太祖变之，今上成之，特远出于唐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1147916_comment'></div>吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1147916_comment'></div>譬之拳石出土，不知嵩、衡、常、泰而后为岳祀也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1147916_comment'></div>飘灰应候，不知杞、梓、栝、柏而后成厦材也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1147916_comment'></div>廉死卑位，应恨不见于此时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1147916_comment'></div>所示文不敢久留，谨以上纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1147916_comment'></div>开白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1147916_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年春</a>　全州任上，招抚溪洞粟氏，作文刻于石。作品：《时鉴》<div id='poem_1147967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147967?labeling=true' target='_blank'>时鉴</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147967")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147967'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147967'>雍熙三年，宜州山夷攻其州弗克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147967_comment'></div>全之西鄙乐安里峒有粟氏固之，会其族南劫兴安县，败入溪峒，连岁不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147967_comment'></div>天子择中贵臣二人，莅全、邵州以静之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147967_comment'></div>明年春，粟氏来归，魁狡皆奉吏州庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147967_comment'></div>乃刻《时鉴》一篇于石以诫之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147967_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1147967'>族盛卑邑，邦大下国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147967_comment'></div>违道致殃，干命取亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147967_comment'></div>居夷邻德，处险近贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147967_comment'></div>蜀难通轺，吴莫容舠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147967_comment'></div>啸万群奸，摧垒倒关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147967_comment'></div>象踣围矣，蛟毙彀已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147967_comment'></div>虿纤曷存，蚁微何奔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147967_comment'></div>虎猛恃力，逼死罔逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147967_comment'></div>隼鸷诚捷，怀饵受緤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147967_comment'></div>小人为美，君子是耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147967_comment'></div>所失若尘，其治如钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147967_comment'></div>宁之弗复，丧乃必覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147967_comment'></div>习礼可式，玩兵竟慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147967_comment'></div>怨惧兴祸，贪欲生过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147967_comment'></div>徇意成朋，怫心见憎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147967_comment'></div>以畏卒溃，苟悦爰萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147967_comment'></div>谨政防乱，慎行避患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147967_comment'></div>缺玉不补，积滓非污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147967_comment'></div>来䊸往亟，愚睽智昵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147967_comment'></div>迹昭事著，利洽动裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147967_comment'></div>平原广野，驰车走马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147967_comment'></div>高浪深渊，有鲔有鳣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147967_comment'></div>保尔攸宜，胥乐在时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147967_comment'></div>刊文无穷，作诫永终。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1147967_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　有文。作品：《讽虞嫔诗》<div id='poem_179337' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179337' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179337?labeling=true' target='_blank'>讽虞嫔诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_179337")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_179337_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179337'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179337'>惟尧则天舜弗复，诞妃冈极恩亭育。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179337'>遏密无闻血盈目，南巡胡为泪染竹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179337'>父轻夫重当何淑，沅湘岸筠烟莓覆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179337'>凝纹叠斑殷郁郁，猿缘鼯号钩辀宿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179337'>朋悽助惋声几哭，剩疑下尤禹湮渎。<div id='poem_sentence_4_179337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_179337'>功充民戴荷百禄，重晖并耀难停毂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_179337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_179337'>元居不宁逝如逐，悲啼负冤生莫卜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_179337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_179337'>卒颠沈澜远昌族，讴讼肇私归永福，柔阴惨尅咎深速。<div id='poem_sentence_7_179337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_179337'>前睇九山排矗矗，到今云颜愁可掬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_179337_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桂林
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5da838ab2f22411fa52dcb3ad2a99ba9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5da838ab2f22411fa52dcb3ad2a99ba9");'><span id='5da838ab2f22411fa52dcb3ad2a99ba9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=991')">990-991年</a>，44-45岁</div><div id='5da838ab2f22411fa52dcb3ad2a99ba9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年秋</a>　由全州移知桂州，有文。作品：《玄风峒铭》<div id='poem_1147960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玄风峒铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147960")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147960'>出桂州东，抵庆林观，背山下有峒出风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147960_comment'></div>淳化元年，开知州事，往避秋暑，因刻铭于峒傍，曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1147960'>桂东丛峰，穴空通风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147960_comment'></div>凄肌森襟，没骨侵心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147960_comment'></div>莹雪若洁，凝冰若冽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147960_comment'></div>暑宇苦燠，周陬流毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147960_comment'></div>其何如斯，为能去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147960_comment'></div>岭山峨峨，岭水汤汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147960_comment'></div>亘古绵今，气炎土荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147960_comment'></div>物爽迩情，候乖朔节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147960_comment'></div>夏雨多凉，秋旱多热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147960_comment'></div>春裘冬扇，朝顺夕变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147960_comment'></div>反倒无恒，夭疠相仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147960_comment'></div>榛莽虫豸，横乱患害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147960_comment'></div>性类所专，造化莫迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147960_comment'></div>我来峒中，百虑时穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147960_comment'></div>翛然自释，忘归终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147960_comment'></div>勒铭岩石，用纪成极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1147960_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年八月八日</a>　作书与同年李巨源。作品：《与朗州李巨源谏议书》<div id='poem_1147919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与朗州李巨源谏议书</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年八月八日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147919")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147919'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147919'>八月八日，开再拜，寓书于朗州谏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147919_comment'></div>历代充时用，为公相侯王，至下群吏，由辞学进士中出以为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147919_comment'></div>同时登第者，指呼为同年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147919_comment'></div>其情爱相视如兄弟，以至子孙累代，莫不为昵比，进相援为显荣，退相累为黜辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147919_comment'></div>君子者成众善，以利民与国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147919_comment'></div>小人者成众恶，以害国与民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147919_comment'></div>耳闻目睹，不越于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147919_comment'></div>太祖皇帝开宝六年，今仆射李公为翰林学士，知礼部贡举事，始有廷试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147919_comment'></div>开幸得与执事于上前登进士第，为同年者二十有六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147919_comment'></div>初仕惟状元宋得校书郎、直史馆，馀遭诸州府置司寇参军选，悉为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147919_comment'></div>到于今十八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147919_comment'></div>其间死者几半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147919_comment'></div>存而居上位者，惟执事特受上知，自谏议大夫得权御史中丞公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147919_comment'></div>宋得入中书省知制诰，复不幸宋病风，废死于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147919_comment'></div>其馀若开辈，如走巅峰，缘危梯，系系不能上、不能下者，其何可俟发白颜颓，壮心殆休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147919_comment'></div>独望执事立朝廷，镇台省，以提以翼，同赞圣君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147919_comment'></div>近闻执事退迁为郎，南逐典郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147919_comment'></div>噫，斯未知下民多尤，将未受其康济耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147919_comment'></div>噫，岂如开辈为同年者，将困焉终极于此耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147919_comment'></div>呜呼，宁视人何易，而自为何难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147919_comment'></div>悲夫，人之处世，多违而少遂，无他知者，不己知也，混混然若雨逐风，鳞逐浪，宁辨其始来而终止也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147919_comment'></div>得为贤，失为愚，其果是而果非乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147919_comment'></div>纪于策，传于口者，详而听之，今昔岂殊远哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147919_comment'></div>大凡祸福进退，君子小人，必以众寡为相胜之道耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147919_comment'></div>譬如鸟兽草木，翔集丛茂，善恶必其类合矣，必其类，疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147919_comment'></div>况朝为荣，暮为辱，岂是己所皆为之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147919_comment'></div>有以直于事而曲于不直于事者，而为己累也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147919_comment'></div>有以免乎近而不免乎远，而为己累也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147919_comment'></div>所好屈之人，而不好屈之于身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147919_comment'></div>好利诸己，而不好利诸彼也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147919_comment'></div>至于相贼害残忍，相族僇毁耻，终不为愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147919_comment'></div>所以古人君子行己有道，正己有方，以礼防之，以信要之，以仁伏之，以义制之，盖畏于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147919_comment'></div>明公度之，是能异于此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147919_comment'></div>朗陵山水清秀，风土稍异岭表，修闲养和，足乐天真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147919_comment'></div>何为冒尘埃，冲风雨，出则畏，处则防，以为己所贵盛耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147919_comment'></div>相去且远，相见未期，珍重自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1147919_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1147919_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年八月八日</a>　是夜，袁姬卒，作哀辞。作品：《袁姬哀辞》<div id='poem_179338' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179338' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179338?labeling=true' target='_blank'>袁姬哀辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年八月八日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_179338")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_179338_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_179338'>袁姬，良家子，父母成都人，开始知宁边军，在阙下娉得姬于其兄。从余来全州、桂州，生二子，一女一男，皆失之。淳化元年，年二十，秋八月八日夜，疾卒于桂州后堂。其念远京师四千里，作哀辞一章，剋石留于桂州。</div><div id='poem_preface_179338_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179338'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179338'>彼美袁姬兮，柔芳懿懿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179338'>瑶沈蕣瘁兮，追惟弗洎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179338'>阴质弱卑兮，资阳望贵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179338'>寿康攸遂兮，夭愆所利。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179338'>北塞南荒兮，偕行万里。<div id='poem_sentence_4_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_179338'>宁期不修兮，溘然而逝。<div id='poem_sentence_5_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_179338'>奔服勤劬兮，丧尔母子。<div id='poem_sentence_6_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_179338'>恫毒我怀兮，摧伤骨髓。<div id='poem_sentence_7_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_179338'>高旻孔仁兮，皇适予委。<div id='poem_sentence_8_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_179338'>明知有生兮，亦必有死。<div id='poem_sentence_9_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_179338'>无如奈何兮，情思罔已。<div id='poem_sentence_10_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_179338'>倏焉胡往兮，音容莫寄。<div id='poem_sentence_11_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_179338'>馀玩遗香兮，忍孰为视。<div id='poem_sentence_12_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_179338'>桂山崭崭兮，翠攒若指。<div id='poem_sentence_13_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_179338'>曷能可忘兮，我心于此。<div id='poem_sentence_14_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_179338'>西流之日兮，东流之水。<div id='poem_sentence_15_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_179338'>瞬息一去兮，终天远矣。<div id='poem_sentence_16_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_179338'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_179338_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_179338'><span class='label'>按：</span>《河东先生集》卷一三。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_179338_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年</a>　与刘昌言书，求其荐用。作品：《与广南西路采访司谏刘昌言书》<div id='poem_1147918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与广南西路采访司谏刘昌言书</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147918")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147918'>唐灭到今一百年，始见太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147918_comment'></div>天子考工较艺，求海内多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147918_comment'></div>尤绝者尽在朝廷，骈骈出头角，群莫能上，开常自叹所不及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147918_comment'></div>以今言之，王著善书，得笔札点画之妙，召置为侍书，日在上左右，出入禁闱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147918_comment'></div>贾玄善奕，专黑白胜负之能，召置为待诏，数数对上争博，坐或穷昼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147918_comment'></div>楚兰善占，得为日者之长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147918_comment'></div>刘翰善药，得为太医之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147918_comment'></div>越有梓匠，得尽能于佛塔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147918_comment'></div>蜀多方士，得逞伎于道术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147918_comment'></div>至于击毬擅场，木射中物，有小奇于类者，皆大显于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147918_comment'></div>盖取其所能，而各尽其所妙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147918_comment'></div>苟不遇上之广求于人，不遗于物，则此数子，果能自异于今乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147918_comment'></div>上所能知其此数子者，必有力言于上，而上始取而择其能，以为用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147918_comment'></div>开所专于古文者三十年矣，始学韩愈氏，传周公、孔子之道，尊尊而亲亲，善善而恶恶，用之即施教化于天下以利万物，不用之即成其书垂之无穷，要其令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147918_comment'></div>开于其儒为文者，庶乎近于古人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147918_comment'></div>比之书、奕、占、药、梓匠、方士翘然出众者，开亦不愧于前数子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147918_comment'></div>而不得如前数子之遇知于上者，盖无其大君子力为开言之于上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147918_comment'></div>所以每常自叹，至于食无味，寝无寐，居不为家，存不为生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147918_comment'></div>尤念其动得谤，行得毁，以谗以害，屈而莫伸之，所为困踬颠沛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147918_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147918_comment'></div>岂为儒不及为他者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147918_comment'></div>此盖上之未尽知于开之所能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147918_comment'></div>前数子皆异端之末，非如开有利国家，活人民，致君如尧禹，立言如典谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147918_comment'></div>用之于兵，战则胜，攻则尅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147918_comment'></div>行之于事，言则中，谋则成，文武之道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147918_comment'></div>彼，上犹知而崇用之，高步阔视，几齿大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147918_comment'></div>若大君子有言开而使上知之者，必以开不下于前数子之为奇特也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147918_comment'></div>明公乘单车，走万里，极炎荒之所僻远，尽耳目之所见闻，为天子别白善恶之于人，必不使开在于前数子之后耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147918_comment'></div>若此时明公不为之言，主上不得而知，即开悲恨为儒不及于为他者也，将终身为终否之人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147918_comment'></div>开再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1147918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年</a>　有文。作品：《湘漓二水说》<div id='poem_1147948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湘漓二水说</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147948")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147948'>湘、漓二水，始一水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147948_comment'></div>出于阳海山，山在桂州兴安县<span class='inlineComment2'>（旧名全义县。）</span>东南九十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147948_comment'></div>西北流至县东五里岭上，始分南北为其二水，北为湘水，南为漓水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147948_comment'></div>求其二水之名于书于记，皆无所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147948_comment'></div>淳化元年，开自全州移知桂州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147948_comment'></div>乘船溯湘水而抵岭下，复以漓水达于桂州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147948_comment'></div>问其岭之名，即分水岭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147948_comment'></div>分水是相离水也，二水异流也，谓其同出阳海，至此岭分南北而离也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147948_comment'></div>二水之名，疑昔人因其水分相离，而乃命之曰湘水也，一水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147948_comment'></div>其北水所为湘，南水所为漓，将有以上下先后而乃名之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147948_comment'></div>水阴属，属北方，北方为水之主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147948_comment'></div>以其北流者归主也，乃尊之，以相字加其名，为上焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147948_comment'></div>又疑为以其北者入于华，南者出于夷，华贵于夷也，故以相字为先焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147948_comment'></div>既二水以二字分名之，即北者为上，为先，名湘也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147948_comment'></div>即离者必加南流者也，所以漓江是分水之南名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147948_comment'></div>因其水之分，名为相离也，乃字傍从水，为湘为漓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147948_comment'></div>凡为字，皆命名者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147948_comment'></div>名者，强称物者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147948_comment'></div>古之以万物错杂，惧难别识也，乃以名各记之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147948_comment'></div>即物之名有类、有假、有义、有因焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147948_comment'></div>斯二水之名，以其水分相离为名，是取类也，是所假也，是从义也，是有因也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147948_comment'></div>今书漓江为「漓」字，疑其不当为此「漓」字也，当以离字傍加水作此「漓」字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147948_comment'></div>又字书古无此「漓」字，酌其理增，而今以为字焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147948_comment'></div>亦由古之他字，皆以义以理撰物者以成字也，非与天地同生于自然耳，亦皆由于人者也，于今悉为世所用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147948_comment'></div>以斯而言之，即古之所为者未必即为是，今之所作者未必即为不是耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147948_comment'></div>凡事亦无古无今焉，惟其为当者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147948_comment'></div>即湘、漓二江之名，孰曰非乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147948_comment'></div>若以其南方为离，流南方为漓江也，即所说之义其疏矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1147948_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年十二月</a>　罢任归京，临行前作新堂铭。作品：《桂州延龄寺西峰僧咸整新堂铭》<div id='poem_1147961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桂州延龄寺西峰僧咸整新堂铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147961")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147961'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147961'>桂州西峰僧咸整，淳化元年，不下山十二年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147961_comment'></div>整之师洎祖师，悉如整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147961_comment'></div>开与赞善大夫张测，为整作新堂以居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147961_comment'></div>有问整之行何为奇者，对曰：若时入阵战贼，勇能进，不顾死者，足为善将矣，况如孙、吴乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147961_comment'></div>交朋间，视其友无欺者，足为义士矣，况如管、鲍乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147961_comment'></div>为政廉以平，足为良吏矣，况如龚、黄乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147961_comment'></div>入朝事君直，能言必尽诚者，足为贤臣矣，况如伊、周乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147961_comment'></div>父兄在，视其室无私者，足为孝子矣，况如曾、颜乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147961_comment'></div>为文理胜辞者，足为大儒矣，况如荀、孟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147961_comment'></div>惟整焦然坐一室，足不践山下寸地，况入豪贵污贱之门，嗃嗃如狗鼠谄窃哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147961_comment'></div>百善万恶，心动即生，身远自藏，几灭半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147961_comment'></div>方之外殊而内同者，止是整能洁其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147961_comment'></div>与之善将之下商较其轻重，整亦足为真僧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147961_comment'></div>由湖湘而南，问僧者，语整为诸先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147961_comment'></div>冬十二月堂成，开诏罢州任，得归阙，留文堂下，为整以铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147961_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1147961'>知生为役兮，无息无利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147961_comment'></div>畏同蹈远兮，出求以异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147961_comment'></div>复本还元兮，尤耽其味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147961_comment'></div>宁如不殊兮，益增乎累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147961_comment'></div>整之专严兮，洁行世世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147961_comment'></div>超然遐迈兮，时谁可洎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147961_comment'></div>穷观永古兮，何足有贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147961_comment'></div>万类千变兮，终焉若是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147961_comment'></div>包极六合兮，未充贪意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147961_comment'></div>精明至止兮，深藏自闭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147961_comment'></div>维堂斯皇兮，犹多馀地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147961_comment'></div>群甡草树兮，藤榛茂翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147961_comment'></div>环邻俯觌兮，胜情与智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147961_comment'></div>祖源师派兮，成流善继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147961_comment'></div>于家于国兮，有惭名位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147961_comment'></div>昼尘夜烛兮，昏嚣若醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147961_comment'></div>城闉岩岫兮，疑画相似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147961_comment'></div>浑沦奔纷兮，孰思而议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147961_comment'></div>跬步天违兮，海赊难既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147961_comment'></div>吁嗟整之兮，离垢脱秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1147961_comment'></div>我宁尔及兮，肠填滓滞。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1147961'></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1147961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年春</a>　由桂州启程返京师。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fcc09d9420184e2caa2ee12f3d6df789_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fcc09d9420184e2caa2ee12f3d6df789");'><span id='fcc09d9420184e2caa2ee12f3d6df789_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年</a>，45岁</div><div id='fcc09d9420184e2caa2ee12f3d6df789' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年闰二月</a>　返京途中，至潭州，作文。作品：《五峰集序》<div id='poem_1147937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147937?labeling=true' target='_blank'>五峰集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（991年闰二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147937")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147937'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147937'>读夫子文章，恨《诗》《书》《礼》《乐》下至《经》遭秦焚毁，各有亡逸，到今求一字语要加于存者，无复可有，况其尽得之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147937_comment'></div>又念汉获壁间科斗书，以编简断裂，巫蛊事起，不能比类寻究，深为痛惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147937_comment'></div>圣人没，其言无得而更闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147937_comment'></div>譬犹登丘望天，远不见者，其何能尽，亦何能知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147937_comment'></div>游秦止陇，宁穷京邑之壮观哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147937_comment'></div>至于他美馀珍，半存半失，心目有爱，曾是无思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147937_comment'></div>淳化二年春，开自桂州诏归京师，遇王次圣自交州使还于衡山廖昼家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147937_comment'></div>次圣，廖之出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147937_comment'></div>廖世善诗，爽于梁朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147937_comment'></div>当马氏有湖湘，得衡，永州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147937_comment'></div>子男十人，图善七言诗，凝善五言诗，立语皆奇拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147937_comment'></div>凝后入江南归李璟，其诗得闻于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147937_comment'></div>图值马之子不嗣，兵兴国乱，多听散坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147937_comment'></div>开因次圣求图诗于昼，得残缺仅百篇，昔人遵度序之为《五峰集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147937_comment'></div>闰月，昼抵潭授余，讽之，篇篇可爱重，恢然言胸臆间事，近世无比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147937_comment'></div>事凡无大也，无小也，能有道，则几乎君子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147937_comment'></div>若图诗，可令人痛其遗逸哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147937_comment'></div>拟之经虽不伦，然观其存而思其亡者，皆必有理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147937_comment'></div>念之足以少见余心也，因之得以及于夫子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147937_comment'></div>意时无贤，将为辞以共叹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147937_comment'></div>时有贤，其如生不能使尽其材，死复丧其事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147937_comment'></div>图，昼祖也，仕马氏为天策府学士、道州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147937_comment'></div>昼之下，学其业者馀十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147937_comment'></div>以是廖之族足为诗家流也。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1147937'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1147937_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年</a>　在潭州，以诗赠僧人梦英。作品：《赠梦英诗》<div id='poem_179340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_179340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/179340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠梦英诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_179340")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_179340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_179340'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_179340'>昼光夜魄阴阳祖，五纬天立五行父。<div id='poem_sentence_0_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_179340'>万灵蕃昌根此树，刚柔各斗清浊聚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_179340'>形类纷然填下土，精英閒见群宁侣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_179340'>雄剧唯神时可主，功格无先明竞睹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_179340'>舍羊犬猪用彪虎，气包茫昧廓区宇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_179340'>刓发披缁心有取，蜕免羁跼脱潜去。<div id='poem_sentence_5_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_179340'>身投西佛学东鲁，尘视诸徒飙远举。<div id='poem_sentence_6_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_179340'>狂呼饱醉贱今古，公室侯庭迎走户。<div id='poem_sentence_7_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_179340'>如攀乔柯腰俯偻，搜经抉诰将完补。<div id='poem_sentence_8_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_179340'>声号大荒铿簨簴，笔诟斯冰卑尔汝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_179340'>戟枝曳阵孰御侮，二十游秦老还楚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_179340'>蛟蟠枯泓骥追鼠，停舟湘濆吾兴语。<div id='poem_sentence_11_179340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_179340'>归返终南恨睽阻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_179340_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

仙桃

-----title
滁州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='494597ad7525479e8f8817cd99a352c3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("494597ad7525479e8f8817cd99a352c3");'><span id='494597ad7525479e8f8817cd99a352c3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=993')">992-993年</a>，46-47岁</div><div id='494597ad7525479e8f8817cd99a352c3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年四月</a>　移滁州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年九月二十五日</a>　作文祭滁州孟玄喆。作品：《祭知滁州孟太师文》<div id='poem_1147981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭知滁州孟太师文</a><span class='authorDate'>（992年九月二十五日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147981")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147981'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147981'>淳化三年九月二十五日，团练副使、金紫光禄大夫、河东县开国男柳开，谨以庶羞清酌之奠，致祭于太师滕国公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147981_comment'></div>太祖神武，开辟区宇，西吞蜀土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147981_comment'></div>公之先王，纳款归疆，以观以亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147981_comment'></div>公魁众嗣，彼居宅贰，来偕奉侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147981_comment'></div>乙丑直岁，邦云殄瘁，于今一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147981_comment'></div>南越滨海，限岭作界，刘亦旋败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147981_comment'></div>金陵跨江，地广物庞，摧城始降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147981_comment'></div>帝圣统乾，兴国纪年，晋垒以颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147981_comment'></div>华往失道，莽然如草，分圻专号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147981_comment'></div>荆潭杭闽，虽据且臣，不讨已宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147981_comment'></div>四征尽来，上恤而哀，仁焉丕哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147981_comment'></div>三家有子，莫踵公趾，或卑而稚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147981_comment'></div>公初届京，虎节龙旌，载锡载行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147981_comment'></div>泰山崇崇，天子命公，爰镇于东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147981_comment'></div>甘陵十载，遗政如在，吏民攸赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147981_comment'></div>去临中山，塞堞闲闲，胡马北还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147981_comment'></div>退假近垣，河流若奔，滑台乃蹲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147981_comment'></div>日出日处，有伸有屈，宁滞乎物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147981_comment'></div>漏停中夜，箕哆南舍，翰飞斯化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147981_comment'></div>惟沸之泉，因流即川，惊波涨天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147981_comment'></div>永阳地僻，褊浅荒斥，公莅养疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147981_comment'></div>适摧高堂，缟衣成行，茅复新丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147981_comment'></div>悠悠难凭，人生可憎，公斯又薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147981_comment'></div>悲今念古，宛如尘聚，风来即去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147981_comment'></div>哗然笑言，倏矣何存，事宁可论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147981_comment'></div>以升即趋，以降即驱，何独异诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147981_comment'></div>开之在谴，公视眷眷，悯予无倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147981_comment'></div>忽然而殂，</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1147981'>然而孤，如饥失哺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147981_comment'></div>惟礼有制，怠之为弃，颓光日逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147981_comment'></div>爱不能留，哀不能收，公其惟休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147981_comment'></div>酒焉在卮，心焉在辞，公知不知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147981_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，伏惟尚享！</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1147981_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=993&endYear=993')">993年年初</a>　以大赦上表太宗乞牵复。作品：《在滁州上陈情表》<div id='poem_1147885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1147885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1147885?labeling=true' target='_blank'>在滁州上陈情表</a><span class='authorDate'>（993年年初）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28421, "北宋", "柳开", "poem_title_1147885")'>柳开</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1147885_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1147885'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1147885'>臣开言：伏以郊天大赦，布陛下至仁之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1147885_comment'></div>率土咸欢，荷陛下无为之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1147885_comment'></div>凡居动植之类，尽承霶霈之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1147885_comment'></div>臣开诚欢诚抃，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1147885_comment'></div>臣于淳化二年，为先知全州日，招唤到粟万延一行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1147885_comment'></div>溪峒公事决，送军人吴忠等上京，在御史台枷禁臣一百二十日，勘责招罪，勒停臣见任崇仪使，追夺臣前任殿中侍御史一任文书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1147885_comment'></div>至淳化三年三月，特蒙圣慈叙用，授臣复州团练副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1147885_comment'></div>至四月，又蒙移授臣滁州团练副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1147885_comment'></div>臣学周公、孔子之道，事唐尧、虞舜之君，孤立无依，薄命多难，但知忠直，不解堤防，致烦宸聪，遂冒朝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1147885_comment'></div>进寸退尺，曾陛下提拔之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1147885_comment'></div>成是败非，感陛下矜容之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1147885_comment'></div>独陛下与臣为主，不似他人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1147885_comment'></div>惟陛下知臣之心，不作私罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1147885_comment'></div>无毫发之赃污，爱屏除其奸讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1147885_comment'></div>况于蛮夷，并系军寨，连群结党，蠹物害民，本期去彼之根源，不谓陷臣于坑阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1147885_comment'></div>郁郁摧出林之秀，铮铮变绕指之柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1147885_comment'></div>一千载逢陛下圣明，二十年蒙陛下养育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1147885_comment'></div>今来退黜，受尽栖迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1147885_comment'></div>得请受则虽有其名，卖折色则并无其价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1147885_comment'></div>惟捋乞丐，以度朝昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1147885_comment'></div>须鬓雪染以浑多，骨肉星散而都尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1147885_comment'></div>陛下如乾坤之高厚，岂不能容微臣之身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1147885_comment'></div>陛下若日月之贞明，岂不能照微臣之意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1147885_comment'></div>雷雨今逢于作解，草木咸庆于惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1147885_comment'></div>仰君亲不报之仁，苏蝼蚁再生之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1147885_comment'></div>东风应候，揭鸡竿而和煦先春；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1147885_comment'></div>北阙如归，拜龙颜而欢呼不日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1147885_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下，念臣已蒙叙用，又经量移，颇困闲官，久居外地，特回睿眷，曲轸圣慈，舍臣已往之非，赐臣牵复之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1147885_comment'></div>臣愿铭肌镂骨，守法奉公，临深履薄以为忧，慎终如始而知诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1147885_comment'></div>规行矩步，不令其厥足用伤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1147885_comment'></div>随波逐流，永保其上善若水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1147885_comment'></div>臣开无任仰天荷圣俟恩，激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1147885_comment'></div>谨奉表陈露以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1147885_comment'></div>臣开诚欢诚抃，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1147885_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1147885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1147885'><span class='label'>按：</span>《河东先生集》卷一○，四部丛刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1147885_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=993&endYear=993')">993年</a>　诏还，得复崇仪使。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
环县

<div class='label1' id='5b75a77c7e104786b0b6ce27552e0b05_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5b75a77c7e104786b0b6ce27552e0b05");'><span id='5b75a77c7e104786b0b6ce27552e0b05_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=993&endYear=993')">993年</a>，47岁</div><div id='5b75a77c7e104786b0b6ce27552e0b05' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=993&endYear=993')">993年</a>　出知环州，平汉蕃市易斗秤，颇得蕃情爱戴。<br /></div>
